Dlg Alliance Chambers 1 Name                                := Alliance Chambers
Dlg Alliance Chambers 1 Descr                               := The Alliance chambers window is used to communicate with the Alliance that you are a member of. Through it you can view the Alliance members and propose new items for the Alliance.
Dlg Alliance Chambers 2 Name                                := Alliance Members List
Dlg Alliance Chambers 2 Descr                               := The list of members that belong to this alliance. Each member is listed with their Empire name, Emperor name, number of votes, and the date they joined the alliance. The number of votes indicates that members weight when voting on new proposals.
Dlg Alliance Chambers 3 Name                                := Current Proposals List
Dlg Alliance Chambers 3 Descr                               := The current proposals list shows all of the items that are up for a vote in front of the alliance. Proposals can include many things from changing the rules of the alliance to adding a new member. Each proposal lists the votes that each member has cast for it, and whether the proposal has passed or not. You can view the specific details of each proposal by selecting it, and selecting the Proposal Details option button.

Dlg Alliance Chambers 4 Descr                               := This section lists general information about the alliance itself such as name, number of members, and the date the alliance was established.

Dlg Alliance Chambers 5 Descr                               := 
Dlg Alliance Chambers 6 Name                                := Quadrant Map

Dlg Colonies 1 Name                                         := Colonies
Dlg Colonies 1 Descr                                        := The Colonies window gives you a complete list of all of the colonies in your empire. With this list you can view all of the attributes of your colonies, filter them, sort them, scrap cargo, or set a colony type.
Dlg Colonies 2 Name                                         := Summary Pane
Dlg Colonies 2 Descr                                        := This section displays summary statistics for your colonies. It displays the number of solar systems where you have colonies, the total number of colonies you have, the number of blockaded colonies, the number of distinct races that inhabit your colonies, and the total population of all of your colonies. In addition, the total research and intelligence points produced per turn are displayed. Below that, the total resources produced by your colonies is displayed. Finally, the maximum resource storage for all of your colonies is displayed.

Dlg Colonies 4 Descr                                        := The list of the colonies is displayed in the center of the window. This list displays all colonies that meet your current Filter criteria. The columns displayed are those that are chosen in the Layout action. You can click on the header for a column to sort the colonies according to that column type. Double-clicking on a particular colony will take you to that colony on the system view. If you click on the header of the picture column, it will change the size of the picture and also the height of each row and allow more rows to be displayed on each screen.

Dlg Combat Piece Options 1 Name                             := Combat Piece Options
Dlg Combat Piece Options 1 Descr                            := The Combat Piece Options window is used to select specific options for the combat piece you have selected in space or ground combat.
Dlg Combat Piece Options 2 Name                             := Options List
Dlg Combat Piece Options 2 Descr                            := The Options list lets you select settings for a specific combat piece. 
Dlg Combat Piece Options 3 Name                             := Use Autotargeting
Dlg Combat Piece Options 3 Descr                            := Determines whether this combat piece will automatically pick targets for its weapons. If this is not selected, you will need to give targeting selections for the piece. If this is selected, then the combat piece will fire on targets based on its current strategy (regardless of what targeting you give it).
Dlg Combat Piece Options 4 Name                             := Use Automove
Dlg Combat Piece Options 4 Descr                            := Determines whether this combat piece will move to the location of its choice. If this is not selected, you will need to give the piece movement orders. If this is selected, then the combat piece will move on its own based on its current strategy (regardless of what orders you give it).
Dlg Combat Piece Options 5 Name                             := Set All Like this
Dlg Combat Piece Options 5 Descr                            := This action sets all combat pieces you own to use these same settings.
Dlg Combat Piece Options 6 Name                             := OK
Dlg Combat Piece Options 6 Descr                            := Set the combat pieces options and closes the window. 
Dlg Combat Piece Options 7 Name                             := Cancel
Dlg Combat Piece Options 7 Descr                            := Ignores any changes you have made and closes the window. 
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 1 Name                          := Combat Simulator Ground
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 1 Descr                         := The Combat Simulator Ground window allows you to simulate ground combat in a safe environment. You can configure the type of planet you fight on, the types of attackers, and the types of defenders. Any combat which takes place in this window is purely simulated and does not affect the rest of your game.
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 2 Name                          := Summary Pane
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 2 Descr                         := This pane displays general information about the combat you have set up. It displays the population of the planet you have selected, the number of facilities, the number of units for the attacker, the number of units for the defender, and the number of empires involved in the combat.
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 3 Name                          := Planet List
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 3 Descr                         := This is a list of planets (that you know of) to use as the simulated location for the ground combat.
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 4 Name                          := Items Present List
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 4 Descr                         := This list presents all of the objects present in combat. The top of the list will typically be the planet you have selected and the simulated owner of the planet. Under the planet is a list of all of the races, units, and facilities that the owner of the planet controls. The end of the list contains a list of the units controlled by the attacking player (the one that is attempting to conquer the planet).
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 5 Name                          := Set Planet
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 5 Descr                         := This action will set the currently selected planet in the Planet List to be the planet used in the combat simulation.
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 6 Name                          := Tactical Combat
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 6 Descr                         := This option indicates that you want to simulate the combat “Tactically”, meaning that you will actually view the battle and control the pieces (using the Combat Tactical – Ground window).

Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 7 Descr                         := This option indicates that you want to simulate the combat “Strategically”, meaning that you will see a high level summary version of the combat (using the Combat Strategic window).

Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 8 Descr                         := This action will display a list of empire for you to choose from. The empire you choose will be the defender (the planet owner).
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 9 Name                          := Set Owner Cargo
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 9 Descr                         := This action will display the Transfer Cargo window so that you can select cargo / units for the defender (the planet owner).
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 10 Name                         := Set Enemy Units
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 10 Descr                        := This action will display the Transfer Cargo window so that you can select units for the attacker.
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 11 Name                         := Place Ground Items
Dlg Combat Simulator Ground 11 Descr                        := This action will display the map of the ground combat and allow you to place the ground units where you want them. This selection is not required for you to play the combat (the ground units are placed automatically), but may be useful if you want to simulate a specific layout of units.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 1 Name                          := Combat Tactical - Space
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 1 Descr                         := The Combat Tactical Space window is displayed when combat occurs and you want to control your ships actions. Combat is in real-time, except that you can control the start and stop of time, and the rate at which is passes. Combat will continue until one side is destroyed, five minutes has passed, or the ships are heading away from each other.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 2 Name                          := Status Bar
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 2 Descr                         := The Status Bar runs along the top of the window.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 5 Name                          := Right-click
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space 5 Descr                         := Right-clicking only has an effect if you currently have a vehicle selected that you own. If you right-click on empty space, then you will give orders to your ship to move to that location. If you right-click on an enemy vehicle, then you will give orders to your ship to target all of its weapons on that vehicle.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 7 Name           := Shields

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 8 Name           := Armor
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 8 Descr          := The current amount of armor remaining out of the total armor that the ship can hold.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 9 Name           := Structure
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 9 Descr          := The current amount of hull structure out of the total hull structure of the ship. If this number reaches zero, then the ship is destroyed.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 10 Name          := Supplies
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 10 Descr         := The current amount of supplies out of the total amount that the ship can hold. When supplies reach zero, weapons can no longer be fired.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 11 Name          := Ordnance
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 11 Descr         := The current amount of ordnance out of the total amount that the ship can hold. When ordnance reaches zero, then weapons which use ordnance will no longer fire.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 12 Name          := Crew
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 12 Descr         := The current amount of crew out of the total crew compliment of the ship. If all of the crew of a ship is killed, then the ship will no longer be under your control.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 13 Name          := Combat Options

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 15 Name          := System Report
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Report Panel 15 Descr         := This action will display the System Report for the system where this combat is taking place. Some systems can have effects on the combat such as negating shields or decreasing speed.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 2 Descr            := The system and sector coordinates where this combat is taking place.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 3 Name             := Combat Time
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 3 Descr            := The game date and specific time of this combat. Time is displayed in hours, minutes, seconds, and milliseconds. As time in combat progresses, the time amount will increase.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 4 Name             := Empires
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 4 Descr            := This section displays the flags of the empires that are taking part in the combat.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 5 Name             := Minimize
Dlg Combat Tactical - Space - Status Bar 5 Descr            := The Minimize button will minimize the entire game so that you can access Windows.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 1 Name                         := Combat Tactical - Ground
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 1 Descr                        := The Combat Tactical Ground window is displayed when combat occurs on a planet’s surface. Combat is in real-time, except that you can control the start and stop of time, and the rate at which is passes. Combat will continue until one side is destroyed or five minutes has passed.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 2 Name                         := Status Bar
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 2 Descr                        := The Status Bar runs along the top of the window.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 3 Name                         := Main Display
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 3 Descr                        := The Main Display shows your current viewpoint on the combat.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 4 Name                         := Left-click
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 4 Descr                        := Left-clicking on a vehicle selects that vehicle. If it’s a vehicle that you control, then you will be able to give orders to it. A report about the selected vehicle will be displayed on the Report Panel.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 5 Name                         := Right-click
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 5 Descr                        := Right-clicking only has an effect if you currently have a vehicle selected that you own. If you right-click on empty space, then you will give orders to your vehicle to move to that location. If you right-click on an enemy vehicle, then you will give orders to your selected vehicle to target all of its weapons on that enemy vehicle.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 6 Name                         := Mouse pointer on the edge of the window
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 6 Descr                        := Moving your mouse pointer to the edge of the screen will scroll the viewpoint in that direction on the map.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 7 Name                         := Scroll Wheel
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 7 Descr                        := Scrolling on the scroll wheel of your mouse will zoom in or zoom out the viewpoint in the Main Display.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 8 Name                         := Overview Map
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 8 Descr                        := The Overview Map displays a high level view of the combat.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 9 Name                         := Report Panel
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 9 Descr                        := The Report Panel displays a report about the currently selected vehicle in the Main Display.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 10 Name                        := Orders Panel
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground 10 Descr                       := The Orders Panel allows you to give orders to the currently selected vehicle in the Main Display.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 1 Name          := Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 1 Descr         := The Report Panel displays information about the currently selected vehicle on the Main Display. You can select any vehicle or building and get a summary report in this display.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 2 Name          := Combat Piece Report
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 2 Descr         := This section displays information about the currently selected vehicle or building. To the left is a portrait of the vehicle, a flag for who owns it, and the name of the vehicle. On the right are details that most vehicles use:
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 3 Name          := Class
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 3 Descr         := The name of the design that this vehicle is based on.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 4 Name          := Size
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 4 Descr         := The name of the size of this vehicle.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 5 Name          := Heading
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 5 Descr         := The angle that this vehicle is heading. 0 degrees is directly up, with angles increasing clockwise from 0 to 360 degrees.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 6 Name          := Speed
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 6 Descr         := The speed at which the vehicle is traveling.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 7 Name          := Shields
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 7 Descr         := The current amount of shield points out of the total that this vehicle generates.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 8 Name          := Armor
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 8 Descr         := The current amount of armor remaining out of the total armor that the vehicle can hold.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 9 Name          := Structure
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 9 Descr         := The current amount of hull structure out of the total hull structure of the vehicle. If this number reaches zero, then the ship is destroyed.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 10 Name         := Supplies
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 10 Descr        := The current amount of supplies out of the total amount that the vehicle can hold. When supplies reach zero, weapons can no longer be fired.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 11 Name         := Ordnance
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 11 Descr        := The current amount of ordnance out of the total amount that the vehicle can hold. When ordnance reaches zero, then weapons which use ordnance will no longer fire.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 12 Name         := Crew
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 12 Descr        := The current amount of crew out of the total crew compliment of the vehicle. If all of the crew of a vehicle is killed, then the vehicle will no longer be under your control.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 13 Name         := Combat Options
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 13 Descr        := This action will display the Combat Options window.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 14 Name         := Item Report
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 14 Descr        := This action will display the Combat Piece Report for this vehicle.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 15 Name         := System Report
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Report Panel 15 Descr        := This action will display the System Report for the system where this combat is taking place. Some systems can have effects on the combat such as negating shields or decreasing speed.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Status Bar 1 Descr           := This panel shows summary details for the combat.

Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Status Bar 2 Descr           := The planet where this combat is taking place.
Dlg Combat Tactical - Ground - Status Bar 3 Name            := Combat Time

Dlg Communicate 1 Name                                      := Communicate
Dlg Communicate 1 Descr                                     := The Communicate window is used to send a message to another empire. The sender needs to select a message type in the Messages List, and then set the specific parameters for the message in the Message Details panel. The sender then sets the Message Tone, and types in the specific text for the message in the Message Text panel. When the message is completed, they press the Send Message button.
Dlg Communicate 2 Name                                      := Summary Pane
Dlg Communicate 2 Descr                                     := The Summary Pane displays information about the entity you are sending the message to. For an empire, this will display the empire flag, empire name, emperor name, and whether we currently have a treaty with that empire, what trade level we have with that empire, and that empire’s mood towards us.
Dlg Communicate 3 Name                                      := Message From Empire
Dlg Communicate 3 Descr                                     := If this message is a reply to a message sent from an empire, then that message is displayed in the Message From Empire panel.
Dlg Communicate 4 Name                                      := Quadrant Map
Dlg Communicate 4 Descr                                     := The Quadrant Map displays your current view of the galaxy.
Dlg Communicate 5 Name                                      := Messages List
Dlg Communicate 5 Descr                                     := The Messages List contains the different message types that you can select from. When creating a message, you need to select a message type first. The message types are grouped into categories such as Proposals, Request / Demand, etc. Once you select a message type from this list, the Message Details pane will change to allow you to set any parameters for this message.
Dlg Communicate 6 Name                                      := Message Details
Dlg Communicate 6 Descr                                     := The Message Details pane allows you to set specific parameters for this message. For example, if you select a message type of Give Gift, then this pane will display the items that are contained in the gift.
Dlg Communicate 7 Name                                      := Message Tone
Dlg Communicate 7 Descr                                     := The Message Tone is an indicator of the mood you are in when sending the message.
Dlg Communicate 8 Name                                      := Message Text
Dlg Communicate 8 Descr                                     := This edit box allows you to type in the specific text for the message. This text will be displayed to the recipient of the message.
Dlg Communicate 9 Name                                      := Set Alliance Rules
Dlg Communicate 9 Descr                                     := This button is only displayed if the message type is Propose New Alliance, Counter Alliance Proposal, or Change Alliance Rule. This button will display the Select Alliance Rules window.
Dlg Communicate 10 Name                                     := Set Treaty Elements
Dlg Communicate 10 Descr                                    := This button is only displayed if the message type is Propose Treaty, Propose Change in Treaty, Counter Treaty Proposal, or Counter Treaty Changes. This button will display the Select Treaty Elements window.
Dlg Communicate 11 Name                                     := Set Give Items
Dlg Communicate 11 Descr                                    := This button is only displayed if the message type is Propose Trade or Counter Trade. This button will display the Select Package window.
Dlg Communicate 12 Name                                     := Set Get Items
Dlg Communicate 12 Descr                                    := This button is only displayed if the message type is Propose Trade or Counter Trade. This button will display the Select Package window.
Dlg Communicate 13 Name                                     := Set Gift Items
Dlg Communicate 13 Descr                                    := This button is only displayed if the message type is Give Gift or Request Gift. This button will display the Select Package window.
Dlg Communicate 14 Name                                     := Start Again
Dlg Communicate 14 Descr                                    := If you wish to clear all of your message settings, press this button. It will clear all of your settings and return the window to the state it was in when you first entered it.
Dlg Communicate 15 Name                                     := Send Message
Dlg Communicate 15 Descr                                    := This action will send the message. If there are any problems with the message, an error dialog will be displayed.
Dlg Communicate 16 Name                                     := Close
Dlg Communicate 16 Descr                                    := This action closes the window. If you have a message in progress, it will cancel the message.
Dlg Comparisons 1 Name                                      := Comparisons
Dlg Comparisons 1 Descr                                     := The Comparisons window allows you to view statistics on all of the empires that you know of.
Dlg Comparisons 2 Name                                      := Empires List
Dlg Comparisons 2 Descr                                     := This list displays all of the empires that you know of including yourself. By pressing the buttons before each empires name, you can select which empires are displayed in the Main Display.
Dlg Comparisons 3 Name                                      := Main Display
Dlg Comparisons 3 Descr                                     := The Main Display shows statistics for all of the empires selected in the Empires List. What information is displayed is determined by the option buttons selected on the right-hand panel.
Dlg Comparisons 4 Name                                      := Scores
Dlg Comparisons 4 Descr                                     := This option causes the Main Display to show historical statistics for all of the empires selected. The information displayed for each empire is its Rank (based on score), the score for the empire (based on the score calculation settings data file), Total Resources, Research Points, Intelligence points, Tech Levels, Total Number of Planets, Total Population, Total Number of Units, Total Ships and Bases. Whether you can view the scores of other empires is based on settings selected in the Game Setup window.
Dlg Comparisons 5 Name                                      := Victory Conditions
Dlg Comparisons 5 Descr                                     := This option displays all of the Victory Conditions selected in the Game Setup window. For each victory condition, a check is shown if each empire has completed the condition.
Dlg Comparisons 6 Name                                      := Graphs
Dlg Comparisons 6 Descr                                     := This option displays a graph of the statistics that can be viewed in the Scores option. The graph displays the statistic over time since the beginning of the game for each empire (with the line in the empire’s color). Of course the statistics may only be shown for empires that you have encountered depending on your game options chosen during set-up. Once this option is selected, several more buttons will be displayed to allow you to select the statistic you want to see graphed.
Dlg Comparisons 7 Name                                      := Select All
Dlg Comparisons 7 Descr                                     := This action will select all of the empires in the Empires List.
Dlg Comparisons 8 Name                                      := Select None
Dlg Comparisons 8 Descr                                     := This action will unselect all of the empires in the Empires List.
Dlg Comparisons 9 Name                                      := Close
Dlg Comparisons 9 Descr                                     := This action closes the window.
Dlg Construction Queues 1 Name                              := Construction Queues
Dlg Construction Queues 1 Descr                             := The Construction Queues window displays all of the constructions queues that you control in your empire. Construction Queues are available for every colony you own, and for each ship that has a Space Yard component on it. Each construction queue can be used to construct new ships, facilities, units, or upgrades. What each construction queue can build is dependent on what kind it is. A colony alone can only build facilities, units, and upgrades. A Space Yard facility is required to build starships and bases. A ship with a space yard component can build other starship or bases.
Dlg Construction Queues 2 Name                              := Summary Pane
Dlg Construction Queues 2 Descr                             := The Summary Pane displays summary information about your empire’s construction queues. The statistics displayed are the total number of construction queues in your empire, the number of planetary construction queues, the number of ship-based construction queues, and the number of queues which are placed on hold. Additional statistics displayed are Net Resources Generated Per Turn (the total resources generated by all of your planets net of maintenance and construction queue usage) and the Construction Queue Usage per Turn (the total resources consumed by your construction queues each turn).
Dlg Construction Queues 3 Name                              := Quadrant Map
Dlg Construction Queues 3 Descr                             := The Quadrant Map displays all of the solar systems you have discovered in the galaxy. When your mouse pointer is over a construction queue in the list, the system where that queue is located is displayed on the map.
Dlg Construction Queues 4 Name                              := Queue List
Dlg Construction Queues 4 Descr                             := The Queue List lists all of the construction queues that meet the current Filter you have selected for the window. Data is arranged in columns (based on the Layout selected) which can be sorted by clicking on the column header above each column. If you double-click an item in the list, it functions the same as clicking the Add To Queue button. If you click on the header of the picture column, it will change the size of the picture and also the height of each row and allow more rows to be displayed on each screen.
Dlg Construction Queues 5 Name                              := Expand Map
Dlg Construction Queues 5 Descr                             := The Expand button expands the Quadrant Map to a larger size.
Dlg Construction Queues 6 Name                              := Layout
Dlg Construction Queues 6 Descr                             := This action will display a list of layouts to choose for this window. The layout determine what information (columns) will be displayed in the list. This action also allows you to create, edit and delete custom layouts where you choose which columns of data will be shown.

Dlg Construction Queues 23 Name                             := Add to Queue
Dlg Construction Queues 23 Descr                            := This action will display the Construction Queue Set window so that you can add or edit the construction items for the currently selected construction queue.
Dlg Construction Queues 24 Name                             := Add To All
Dlg Construction Queues 24 Descr                            := This action will display the Construction Queue Set window so that you can add new construction items to all of the construction queues that are currently selected in the list.
Dlg Construction Queues 25 Name                             := Add To Fastest
Dlg Construction Queues 25 Descr                            := This action will display the Construction Queue Set window so that you can add new construction items to the construction queues that are currently selected in the list. The new construction items will be added to the selected queues in order by which queue will get the item done fastest. Think of this as spreading a number of constructions over a group of queues so that they will get done as fast as possible.
Dlg Construction Queues 26 Name                             := Upgrade Facilities
Dlg Construction Queues 26 Descr                            := This action will add upgrade construction items to all of your construction queues to upgrade facilities on your colonies. Only colonies that have facilities which can be upgraded will get new items.
Dlg Construction Queues 27 Name                             := Scrap Cargo
Dlg Construction Queues 27 Descr                            := This action will allow you to select cargo to be scrapped on the currently selected construction queues.

Dlg Construction Queues 28 Descr                            := This action will close the window.
Dlg Construction Queues 29 Name                             := Total Construction Queues
Dlg Construction Queues 29 Descr                            := The total number of planet and ship born construction queues that you have. All colonies and each ship with a space yard have construction queues. 
Dlg Construction Queues 30 Name                             := Planetary Construction Queues
Dlg Construction Queues 30 Descr                            := The number of colonies that you own that can construct items.
Dlg Construction Queues 31 Name                             := Ship Construction Queues
Dlg Construction Queues 31 Descr                            := The number of ships that you own which have working space yards on them. 
Dlg Construction Queues 32 Name                             := Queues On Hold
Dlg Construction Queues 32 Descr                            := The number of construction queues that you have placed on hold. 
Dlg Construction Queues 33 Name                             := Net Resources Generated Per Turn
Dlg Construction Queues 33 Descr                            := The total number of resources your treasury will gain each turn. Net Resources are computed as the total your colonies generate plus trade plus tariffs plus remote mining, minus tariffs against you minus maintenance costs minus the amount your construction queues are consuming. 
Dlg Construction Queues 34 Name                             := Construction Queue Usage Per Turn
Dlg Construction Queues 34 Descr                            := The total number of resources per turn that all of your construction queues consume.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 1 Name                           := Construction Queue Set
Dlg Construction Queue Set 1 Descr                          := The Construction Queue Set window allows you to add new construction items to a construction queue.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 2 Name                           := Summary Pane
Dlg Construction Queue Set 2 Descr                          := The Summary Pane shows summary information for the current construction queue. A picture of the ship or planet is displayed, then its name, cargo space remaining out of total, and what types of items this construction queue can build. Also displayed is the current construction rate for this construction queue. This is the amount of resources that can be used per turn by the construction queue. So if an item costs a total of 10,000 minerals, and the queue rate is 2000 minerals per turn, the item will take 5 turns to complete.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 3 Name                           := Quadrant Map
Dlg Construction Queue Set 3 Descr                          := The Quadrant Map displays all of the solar systems that your empire has discovered. The system where this construction queue is located is highlighted on the map.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 4 Name                           := Available Items List
Dlg Construction Queue Set 4 Descr                          := The Available Items List displays all of the possible items that you can construct. The list displays either Facilities, Ships (actually ship designs), Units (unit designs), and Upgrades.  Each row shows the item’s picture, its name, its cost in resources, the time it will take to construct at this construction queue, the size in kT of this item (cargo space), how many of the item are currently in existence in this system (out of your whole empire), and how many are currently in queues in this system waiting to be built (out of your whole empire). Double clicking an item will add it to the construction queue list. You can also select an item and press the Add Item button.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 5 Name                           := Construction Queue List
Dlg Construction Queue Set 5 Descr                          := The Construction Queue List displays all of the items that are waiting to be built by this construction queue. The items are listed in the order that they will be worked on. Each item shows its picture, name, how many of these items to build, and how much time it will take to build this item. The time only applies once the items higher in the list have been completed.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 6 Name                           := Expand Map
Dlg Construction Queue Set 6 Descr                          := This action will expand the quadrant map to a larger size.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 7 Name                           := Facilities
Dlg Construction Queue Set 7 Descr                          := This option will show facilities to construct in the Available Items List.

Dlg Construction Queue Set 8 Descr                          := This option will show ship designs to construct in the Available Items List.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 9 Name                           := Units
Dlg Construction Queue Set 9 Descr                          := This option will show unit designs to construct in the Available Items List.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 10 Name                          := Upgrades
Dlg Construction Queue Set 10 Descr                         := This option will show upgrades to construct in the Available Items List. Upgrades are to upgrade an old facility on a planet to a newer version.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 11 Name                          := Amount
Dlg Construction Queue Set 11 Descr                         := Amount is the number of items to construct when an item is added to the list. Use the Plus and Minus buttons to change this amount, or click on the amount and type in a new number.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 12 Name                          := Add Item
Dlg Construction Queue Set 12 Descr                         := Pressing this button will add the currently selected item in the Available Items List to the Construction Queue List. The amount added is based on the Amount setting.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 13 Name                          := Remove Item
Dlg Construction Queue Set 13 Descr                         := Pressing this button will remove the currently selected item in the Construction Queue List.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 14 Name                          := Clear Items
Dlg Construction Queue Set 14 Descr                         := Pressing this button will remove all items from the Construction Queue List.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 15 Name                          := Reorder Items
Dlg Construction Queue Set 15 Descr                         := This button will display a reordering dialog so that you can reorder the items in the Construction Queue List. Keep in mind that the items in the list are worked on in order from top to bottom.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 16 Name                          := Fill From Item List
Dlg Construction Queue Set 16 Descr                         := This action will allow you to fill the Construction Queue List for a predefined list of construction items. This action will remove any items that are currently in the list.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 17 Name                          := Create Item List
Dlg Construction Queue Set 17 Descr                         := This action will create an Item List template from the items currently in the Construction Queue List. The items will be stored under a name you define so that you can quickly fill later queues with these same items.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 18 Name                          := Queue Settings
Dlg Construction Queue Set 18 Descr                         := This action displays the Queues settings window. This window will allow you to change the settings for this construction queue. Settings include “On Hold” which will put this queue on hold so that is does not construct any further items. “Emergency Build” is a setting which will cause your construction queue to build items 50% faster. This emergency status can only last a maximum of 10 turns. Once the time is up, or the status is turned off, the queue will be in “Slow Build” for as many turns it was in emergency build. “Slow Build” means that the construction queue will build at 25% of its normal rate. “Repeat Build” indicates that construction queue should endlessly cycle through the list building the items. Normally items are removed from the list once they are constructed. Repeat build keeps the items in the list and cycles through all of them.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 19 Name                          := Close
Dlg Construction Queue Set 19 Descr                         := This action closes the window.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 20 Name                          := Move Item Up
Dlg Construction Queue Set 20 Descr                         := Moves the currently selected queue item up one place. 
Dlg Construction Queue Set 21 Name                          := Move Item Down
Dlg Construction Queue Set 21 Descr                         := Moves the currently selected queue item down one place. 
Dlg Construction Queue Set 22 Name                          := Done
Dlg Construction Queue Set 22 Descr                         := Indicates that you are done reordering the construction queue. The button panel will return to normal after this. 
Dlg Construction Queue Set 23 Name                          := Portrait
Dlg Construction Queue Set 23 Descr                         := A picture of this construction queue object be it ship or planet.
Dlg Construction Queue Set 24 Name                          := Queue Name
Dlg Construction Queue Set 24 Descr                         := The name of the object that can construct items.

Dlg Construction Queue Set 29 Descr                         := YES or NO whether this construction queue can build units.

Dlg Controls Window 1 Name                                  := Controls Window
Dlg Controls Window 1 Descr                                 := The Controls window allows you to view and change the specific hotkeys used in the game.
Dlg Controls Window 2 Name                                  := Category List
Dlg Controls Window 2 Descr                                 := The Category List displays the categories of hotkeys used in the game. When you select a specific category in the list, the Keys List will display all of the keys within that category.
Dlg Controls Window 3 Name                                  := Keys List
Dlg Controls Window 3 Descr                                 := The Keys List displays the various hotkeys used in the game for the selected category. Each keys lists its name and an edit box with the key combination. To change a key combination merely click on the edit box and type in a new hotkey.
Dlg Controls Window 4 Name                                  := Default
Dlg Controls Window 4 Descr                                 := The Default button will cause all of the hotkeys to be reset to their original settings. Any changes you have made to the hotkeys will be lost.

Dlg Controls Window 5 Descr                                 := This button closes the window and saves any changes you have made.
Dlg Convert Resources 1 Name                                := Convert Resources
Dlg Convert Resources 1 Descr                               := The Convert Resources window allows you to select resources to convert from one type to another.
Dlg Convert Resources 2 Name                                := Conversion Types List
Dlg Convert Resources 2 Descr                               := The Conversion Types List displays the various conversions that can be selected. Select from the list the type of conversion you wish to perform.
Dlg Convert Resources 3 Name                                := Conversions To Perform List
Dlg Convert Resources 3 Descr                               := The Conversions to Perform List displays all of the conversions that you wish to execute. Each item will list the original resource type and how many resources you wish to convert, and the new type of resource they will become and the final amount after conversion. These conversions will not actually occur until you press the OK button.
Dlg Convert Resources 4 Name                                := Convert
Dlg Convert Resources 4 Descr                               := The Convert button will add the currently selected Conversion Type selected to the Conversions to Perform List. The amount to convert is selected in the Amount box. You can add as many conversions as you like, but keep in mind that there is typically a loss in resources for each conversion.
Dlg Convert Resources 5 Name                                := Amount
Dlg Convert Resources 5 Descr                               := The Amount display shows how many resources you wish to convert when pressing the Convert button.
Dlg Convert Resources 6 Name                                := Cancel Convert
Dlg Convert Resources 6 Descr                               := The Cancel Convert button will cancel the currently selected item in the Conversions To Perform List.
Dlg Convert Resources 7 Name                                := OK
Dlg Convert Resources 7 Descr                               := This action will execute the conversions listed in the Conversions To Perform List and then close the window.
Dlg Convert Resources 8 Name                                := Cancel
Dlg Convert Resources 8 Descr                               := This action will cancel the selected conversions and close the window.
Dlg Convert Resources 9 Name                                := Plus Button
Dlg Convert Resources 9 Descr                               := Increase the Amount To Add by a factor of 10. 
Dlg Convert Resources 10 Name                               := Minus Button
Dlg Convert Resources 10 Descr                              := Decrease the Amount To Add by a factor of 10. 
Dlg Designs 1 Name                                          := Designs
Dlg Designs 1 Descr                                         := Vehicle Designs are templates on which ships or units are created. Once you have a design for a ship or unit, you can add that design to a construction queue to create an actual vehicle of that type.
Dlg Designs 2 Name                                          := Summary Panel
Dlg Designs 2 Descr                                         := The Summary Panel displays statistical information for your designs and for the currently selected design. Empire wide statistics are Number of Ship Designs, Number of Base Designs, Number of Unit Designs, Number of Enemy Ship Designs, Number of Enemy Base Designs, and Number of Enemy Unit Designs. Statistics specific to the currently selected design are the Design Name, Number Constructed, Number In Service, Number Destroyed, Number Scrapped, and Enemy Tonnage Destroyed.
Dlg Designs 3 Name                                          := Designs List
Dlg Designs 3 Descr                                         := The Designs Lists displays all of the designs that match your current Filter criteria. The designs are grouped according to design type, and each design shows a picture of its vehicle size and its name. When you select a design from the list, its details will be displayed in the middle of the window.
Dlg Designs 4 Name                                          := Design Details
Dlg Designs 4 Descr                                         := The Design Details panel is actually a display of the Design Report window for the currently selected design in the Designs List. See the Report – Vehicle Design window for more details on this display.
Dlg Designs 5 Name                                          := Filter
Dlg Designs 5 Descr                                         := This action will display a list of filters for you to choose from. The filters dictate what kinds of designs will be displayed in the Designs List.
Dlg Designs 6 Name                                          := Our Non-Obsolete Ship Designs
Dlg Designs 6 Descr                                         := Only non-obsolete ship designs we created will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 7 Name                                          := Our Non-Obsolete Unit Designs
Dlg Designs 7 Descr                                         := Only non-obsolete unit designs we created will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 8 Name                                          := Our Ship Designs
Dlg Designs 8 Descr                                         := All ship designs we created will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 9 Name                                          := Our Unit Designs
Dlg Designs 9 Descr                                         := All unit designs we created will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 10 Name                                         := Enemy Ship Designs
Dlg Designs 10 Descr                                        := All enemy ship designs we have encountered will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 11 Name                                         := Enemy Unit Designs
Dlg Designs 11 Descr                                        := All enemy unit designs we have encountered will be displayed.
Dlg Designs 12 Name                                         := Create
Dlg Designs 12 Descr                                        := This action will allow you to create a new design. Once selected, a window will be displayed for you to choose what kind of vehicle you want to create such as Ship, Base, Unit, etc. After that, you will be asked to pick a vehicle size from the Select Vehicle Size window. Finally, the Design Create window will be displayed to allow you to create the design.
Dlg Designs 13 Name                                         := Edit
Dlg Designs 13 Descr                                        := Edit will allow you to edit the currently selected design in the Designs List. You can only edit a design if you have never actually constructed a vehicle from that design. This action will display the Design Create window for the actual editing.
Dlg Designs 14 Name                                         := Copy
Dlg Designs 14 Descr                                        := Copy will allow you to make a new design starting from a copy of the currently selected design in the Designs List. The Design Create window will be displayed with the copy that you can edit and save.
Dlg Designs 15 Name                                         := Upgrade
Dlg Designs 15 Descr                                        := The Upgrade action is much like the Copy action except that the copy will have all of its components upgraded to the latest level you have access to. The Design Create window will be displayed so that you may edit and save the new design. If you are using a design name such as "Attack Ship Mk I," the upgraded version will automatically be named "Attack Ship Mk II."
Dlg Designs 16 Name                                         := Make Obsolete
Dlg Designs 16 Descr                                        := This action will mark the currently selected design in the Designs List as obsolete. Marking a design as obsolete is useful so that you differentiate between designs you still use and those you don’t. Obsolete designs are not shown in the Construction Queue Set window to be constructed. You can mark and unmark a design anytime you want.
Dlg Designs 17 Name                                         := Set Strategy
Dlg Designs 17 Descr                                        := This action will display a list of strategies for you to pick from for the currently selected design in the Designs List. A strategy is used by your vehicle when the ship is in combat under computer control. A strategy defines how a ship moves and targets its weapons.
Dlg Designs 18 Name                                         := Space Simulator
Dlg Designs 18 Descr                                        := This action will display the Combat Simulator Space window so that you can perform a combat simulation with your designs.
Dlg Designs 19 Name                                         := Ground Simulator
Dlg Designs 19 Descr                                        := This action will display the Combat Simulator Ground window so that you can perform a combat simulation with your designs.
Dlg Designs 20 Name                                         := Close
Dlg Designs 20 Descr                                        := Closes this window.
Dlg Designs 21 Name                                         := Number of Ship Designs
Dlg Designs 21 Descr                                        := The total number of ship designs that you have created.
Dlg Designs 22 Name                                         := Number of Base Designs
Dlg Designs 22 Descr                                        := The total number of base designs that you have created.
Dlg Designs 23 Name                                         := Number of Unit Designs
Dlg Designs 23 Descr                                        := The total number of unit designs that you have created.
Dlg Designs 24 Name                                         := Number of Enemy Ship Designs
Dlg Designs 24 Descr                                        := The total number of enemy ship designs that you have encountered in combat.
Dlg Designs 25 Name                                         := Number of Enemy Base Designs
Dlg Designs 25 Descr                                        := The total number of enemy base designs that you have encountered in combat.
Dlg Designs 26 Name                                         := Number of Enemy Unit Designs
Dlg Designs 26 Descr                                        := The total number of enemy unit designs that you have encountered in combat.
Dlg Designs 27 Name                                         := Design Name
Dlg Designs 27 Descr                                        := The name of the currently selected design.
Dlg Designs 28 Name                                         := Number Constructed
Dlg Designs 28 Descr                                        := The amount of vehicles constructed from the currently selected design.
Dlg Designs 29 Name                                         := Number In Service
Dlg Designs 29 Descr                                        := The amount of vehicles that are currently in service using the currently selected design.
Dlg Designs 30 Name                                         := Number Destroyed
Dlg Designs 30 Descr                                        := The amount of vehicles that have been destroyed which used the currently selected design.
Dlg Designs 31 Name                                         := Number Scrapped
Dlg Designs 31 Descr                                        := The number of vehicles of the currently selected design that you have scrapped. 
Dlg Designs 32 Name                                         := Enemy Tonnage Destroyed
Dlg Designs 32 Descr                                        := The total enemy tonnage that vehicles of this design have destroyed. 
Dlg Designs 33 Name                                         := Upgrade Queues
Dlg Designs 33 Descr                                        := This action will upgrade an old design in your construction queues to a newer design. First select a design in the designs list, then press this button. A new window will display a list of designs that are not obsolete, of the same vehicle type (ship, fighter, satellite, etc.), and of the same general type (Attack Ship, Defense Ship, etc.) Once you select a design and press OK, all currently queued old designs will be changed to the new design, as long as work has not started on the item. 
Dlg Design Create 1 Name                                    := Design Create
Dlg Design Create 1 Descr                                   := When creating a design, you will go through the following process. First you will select the vehicle type such as Ship, Base, Unit, etc. Then you will select a size for your vehicle. At this point you will be on this window and ready to create your design. The main portion of creating your design is adding components to your vehicle layout. Most vehicles will need a control center like a Bridge, Life Support, and Crew Quarters. A ship will also need engines, weapons, sensors, armor, shields, supply storage, and ordnance storage. These components are picked up from the Available Components List and then placed on your vehicle layout. Once all of the warnings in the Warnings list are removed, then your design can be created.
Dlg Design Create 2 Name                                    := Design Statistics Panel
Dlg Design Create 2 Descr                                   := The Designs Statistics panel is the main information panel about your design. Clicking anywhere in the statistics window will flip the page and allow you to view additional statistics.
Dlg Design Create 3 Name                                    := Name
Dlg Design Create 3 Descr                                   := The name of this design. Until you select a name this will list “None”. You can select a design name by pressing the Set Design Name button. Upgraded ships may have a new name automatically appended to them if you are using certain design name configurations such as "Attack Ship Mk I."
Dlg Design Create 4 Name                                    := Vehicle Type
Dlg Design Create 4 Descr                                   := The type of vehicle that this is such as Ship, Base, Troop, Fighter, etc.
Dlg Design Create 5 Name                                    := Vehicle Size
Dlg Design Create 5 Descr                                   := The name of the size of this vehicle.
Dlg Design Create 6 Name                                    := Design Type
Dlg Design Create 6 Descr                                   := The design type for this design. The design type is a designation that you set by pressing the Select Design Type button. The design type designation is just a way for you to classify your design such as Attack Ship, Colonizing Ship, etc.
Dlg Design Create 7 Name                                    := Strategy
Dlg Design Create 7 Descr                                   := The name of the strategy selected for this design. You can set this by pressing the Set Strategy button.
Dlg Design Create 8 Name                                    := Tonnage Used
Dlg Design Create 8 Descr                                   := The amount of tonnage space used on this design out of the total available. Each component you place on the design will add to the tonnage space total. You cannot use more tonnage space than is available.
Dlg Design Create 9 Name                                    := Total Cost
Dlg Design Create 9 Descr                                   := The total cost in resources for this design. The total cost is calculated as the resource cost for the vehicle size, plus the resource costs for all of the components placed on it.
Dlg Design Create 10 Name                                   := Hull Structure
Dlg Design Create 10 Descr                                  := The tonnage hull structure of this design. The hull structure is how much damage this vehicle can take before it is destroyed.
Dlg Design Create 11 Name                                   := Cargo Space
Dlg Design Create 11 Descr                                  := The amount of cargo space on this vehicle.
Dlg Design Create 12 Name                                   := Movement
Dlg Design Create 12 Descr                                  := The number of movement points for this vehicle. Each engine you add to the design will add an additional movement point up to a maximum for the vehicle size. Each movement point is equal to 1 sector that this vehicle can move each turn.
Dlg Design Create 13 Name                                   := Shields
Dlg Design Create 13 Descr                                  := The number of shield points that this vehicle will generate.
Dlg Design Create 14 Name                                   := Crew Capacity
Dlg Design Create 14 Descr                                  := The number of crew members needed to operate this vehicle.
Dlg Design Create 15 Name                                   := Supply Capacity
Dlg Design Create 15 Descr                                  := The amount of supply that this vehicle can carry. Supply is the fuel and power for this vehicle. When your supplies run out, your ship will be out of power.
Dlg Design Create 16 Name                                   := Ordnance Capacity
Dlg Design Create 16 Descr                                  := The amount of ordnance that this vehicle can carry. Ordnance is the ammo used by some of your weapons.
Dlg Design Create 17 Name                                   := Component Mounts
Dlg Design Create 17 Descr                                  := The Components Mounts list will list any component mounts that you have discovered. You can select a mount in the list to use it for the weapons that you add to your design (if applicable). A component mount is a holder for the component which enhances its abilities. Mounts can increase the damage and range for weapons.
Dlg Design Create 18 Name                                   := Available Components
Dlg Design Create 18 Descr                                  := The Available Components List displays all of the components that are available for use on your designs. Only those components which meet your selected filter criteria will be displayed. You can click on a component in this list to pick it up and then place it on the design layout. You can also drop a component on this list to get rid of it so that you can pick up another one. Pressing the shift key while placing a component keeps that component selected to place it in additional slots. Pressing the shift key while clicking on a component already placed on the design will remove that component.
Dlg Design Create 19 Name                                   := Design Layout
Dlg Design Create 19 Descr                                  := The Design Layout is a top down perspective on the components on your design. A single component can be placed in each box in the layout. You can click on a component in the available components list to pick it up and then click again in a box in the layout to place it. You can perform the reverse to remove a component from your layout. Pressing the shift key while placing a component keeps that component selected to place it in additional slots. Pressing the shift key while clicking on a component already placed on the design will remove that component.
Dlg Design Create 20 Name                                   := You can also hold the Shift key when placing a component to keep the component selected to add it multiple times to your design layout. If you hold Shift while clicking a component already on your design layout, this will remove the component from the design layout. You can also right click on any component to get a detailed report on that component.
Dlg Design Create 20 Descr                                  := You’ll notice that boxes have a letter in the top right corner of either “O”, “I”, or “A”, and “A” boxes have a red border. The letter indicates whether this location is in the Outer Hull, Inner Hull, or Armor section of the vehicle. Any kind of component can be placed in the Outer Hull or Inner Hull, but only Armor components can be placed in the Armor section. The sections indicate the order in which components will be damaged on your design. When your vehicle takes damage (after any shields are depleted), components in the Armor section are damaged first, then components in the Outer Hull are damaged, and finally components in the Inner Hull are damaged.
Dlg Design Create 21 Name                                   := Warnings List
Dlg Design Create 21 Descr                                  := The Warnings List displays all of the warnings for this design. A warning is a requirement that you have to satisfy before the design can be completed. If there are no warnings shown, then you can create your design. For example, if you put too many components on your design, a warning will display saying that you have used too much tonnage space on the design.
Dlg Design Create 22 Name                                   := Auto Complete
Dlg Design Create 22 Descr                                  := This action will cause the computer to generate your design for you. It will clear any existing components, and other design information, and then add components based on the design type of the vehicle. 
Dlg Design Create 23 Name                                   := Upper Decks
Dlg Design Create 23 Descr                                  := There are three decks for every design. This option button lets you select between the three decks that are displayed in the Design Layout.
Dlg Design Create 24 Name                                   := Middle Decks
Dlg Design Create 24 Descr                                  := This option displays the middle deck of the design.
Dlg Design Create 25 Name                                   := Lower Decks
Dlg Design Create 25 Descr                                  := This option displays the lower deck of the design.
Dlg Design Create 26 Name                                   := Filter Comps
Dlg Design Create 26 Descr                                  := The Filter Comps button will display a list of filters to use on the Available Components List. Only those components which are in the filter category selected will be displayed in the list.
Dlg Design Create 27 Name                                   := Select Ship Size
Dlg Design Create 27 Descr                                  := This action will display the Select Vehicle Size window for you to choose a size for this design. Changing the vehicle size on an existing design will remove all of the components you have placed on the design layout.
Dlg Design Create 28 Name                                   := Select Design Type
Dlg Design Create 28 Descr                                  := This action will display a list of design types for you to choose for this design. The design type is a general designation that you choose to help categorize your vehicles.
Dlg Design Create 29 Name                                   := Set Design Name
Dlg Design Create 29 Descr                                  := This action will display a list of design names for you to choose for this design. Besides choosing a name from the list, you can also type in a new name. Every design for you empire has to have a unique name.
Dlg Design Create 30 Name                                   := Set Strategy
Dlg Design Create 30 Descr                                  := Set Strategy will display a list of strategies for you to choose for this design. Strategies can be modified under Empire Options.
Dlg Design Create 31 Name                                   := Clear Design
Dlg Design Create 31 Descr                                  := This action will clear your design and set it back to an empty state.
Dlg Design Create 32 Name                                   := Weapons Report
Dlg Design Create 32 Descr                                  := The Weapons Report will display the Weapons Grid window. This window is very useful in comparing weapons that you have discovered so that you can pick the most appropriate ones for your design.
Dlg Design Create 33 Name                                   := Create
Dlg Design Create 33 Descr                                  := This action will create your design and close the window. Your design can only be saved if all of the Warnings have been removed.
Dlg Design Create 34 Name                                   := Cancel
Dlg Design Create 34 Descr                                  := This action will cancel your design and close the window.
Dlg Design Create 35 Name                                   := Next Page
Dlg Design Create 35 Descr                                  := This button will toggle between the display of two different sets of design statistics. 
Dlg Design Create 36 Name                                   := Attack
Dlg Design Create 36 Descr                                  := The attack bonus for this vehicle in combat. The higher the number, the better the chance that this vehicle will hit enemy vehicles with its direct-fire weapons.
Dlg Design Create 37 Name                                   := Defense
Dlg Design Create 37 Descr                                  := The defense bonus for this vehicle in combat. The higher the number, the more difficult it is for enemy ships to hit this vehicle with direct-fire weapons.
Dlg Design Create 38 Name                                   := Turn Rate
Dlg Design Create 38 Descr                                  := The rate at which this vehicle can turn to a new heading in combat. 
Dlg Design Create 39 Name                                   := Acceleration
Dlg Design Create 39 Descr                                  := The rate at which this vehicle can change its speed in combat. 
Dlg Display Setup 1 Name                                    := Display Setup
Dlg Display Setup 1 Descr                                   := The Display Setup window allows you configure graphics setup options for the game.
Dlg Display Setup 2 Name                                    := Display Driver
Dlg Display Setup 2 Descr                                   := The current display driver in use. This display driver is the graphics card or adapter you use for the display.
Dlg Display Setup 3 Name                                    := Video Mode
Dlg Display Setup 3 Descr                                   := The Video Mode is the resolution and color depth used for the game.
Dlg Display Setup 4 Name                                    := 3D Device
Dlg Display Setup 4 Descr                                   := The 3D Device is the 3D adapter used for graphics display in the game.
Dlg Display Setup 5 Name                                    := Video Memory Usage
Dlg Display Setup 5 Descr                                   := Video Memory Usage can be either “Auto” or “Safe”. The “Auto” selection is the default and should be used unless you run into a problem with the display. If you do have a problem, try setting this to “Safe” to see if the problem is fixed.
Dlg Display Setup 6 Name                                    := Graphic Detail
Dlg Display Setup 6 Descr                                   := The Graphic Detail is the level of detail used for graphics in the game. The higher the setting the more detailed the graphics are but the slower the display will be. If you find that the display is to slow (that you are getting a low FPS rate), try setting this to a lower setting.
Dlg Display Setup 7 Name                                    := Background Detail
Dlg Display Setup 7 Descr                                   := The Background Detail is the level of detail in the background environment. Like Graphic Detail, if you find that your game is running slowly, try setting this to a lower setting.
Dlg Display Setup 8 Name                                    := Change Display Driver
Dlg Display Setup 8 Descr                                   := This action displays a window which allows you to choose a new display driver.
Dlg Display Setup 9 Name                                    := Change Video Mode
Dlg Display Setup 9 Descr                                   := This action displays a window which allows you to choose a new video mode.
Dlg Display Setup 10 Name                                   := Change 3D Device
Dlg Display Setup 10 Descr                                  := This action displays a window which allows you to choose a new 3D Device.
Dlg Display Setup 11 Name                                   := Change Video Memory Usage
Dlg Display Setup 11 Descr                                  := This action toggles the Video Memory Usage setting.
Dlg Display Setup 12 Name                                   := Change Graphic Detail
Dlg Display Setup 12 Descr                                  := This action toggles the Graphic Detail setting.
Dlg Display Setup 13 Name                                   := Change Background Detail
Dlg Display Setup 13 Descr                                  := This action toggles the Background Detail setting.
Dlg Display Setup 14 Name                                   := Close
Dlg Display Setup 14 Descr                                  := Closes the window and saves your settings.
Dlg Empires 1 Name                                          := Empires
Dlg Empires 1 Descr                                         := The Empires window displays all of the Empires that you have encountered in the galaxy. Through this window you can communicate with other empires and view status reports on them.
Dlg Empires 2 Name                                          := Known Empires List
Dlg Empires 2 Descr                                         := This is a list of all of the empires that you have encountered in the game. Each empire is listed with its flag, the name of the empire, the name of its emperor, if you have a treaty with that empire, and their current mood. By selecting an empire in this list, you can display details about them in the center of the window.
Dlg Empires 3 Name                                          := Empire Details
Dlg Empires 3 Descr                                         := The Empire Details section displays summary details about the empire selected in the Empires List. The portrait of the main empire’s race is displayed, along with the empire name, its flag, its home planet type, atmosphere breathed, and their ship style. Also listed is any current treaty that we have with that empire, what trade percentage we have with them, and their current mood towards us. The list section displays details based on the option selected on the right panel.
Dlg Empires 4 Name                                          := Quadrant Map
Dlg Empires 4 Descr                                         := The Quadrant Map displays the solar systems that we have discovered.
Dlg Empires 5 Name                                          := Expand Map
Dlg Empires 5 Descr                                         := Pressing this button will expand the Quadrant Map to a larger size.
Dlg Empires 6 Name                                          := Our Treaty Elements
Dlg Empires 6 Descr                                         := This option will display the current treaty elements we have with this empire in the center list. This option will only display items if we currently have a treaty with the empire.
Dlg Empires 7 Name                                          := Estimates
Dlg Empires 7 Descr                                         := This option will display our rough estimates of the size and strength of this empire. Our estimate gets better based on our relation with that empire and our intelligence level.
Dlg Empires 8 Name                                          := Technology
Dlg Empires 8 Descr                                         := This option displays all of the known technologies that we believe this empire possesses.
Dlg Empires 9 Name                                          := Other Relations
Dlg Empires 9 Descr                                         := This option displays the relations with other empires that this empire is currently in. We will only know of the relations if we have a treaty with them, or if we have discovered it through intelligence operations. Relations are displayed as: (None), War, or a specific treaty type is listed.
Dlg Empires 10 Name                                         := Messages
Dlg Empires 10 Descr                                        := This option displays any messages that have been sent to us from this empire. These are the same messages as are displayed in the Log Window. You can reply to the messages here by hitting the Replay button in the list.
Dlg Empires 11 Name                                         := Empire Report
Dlg Empires 11 Descr                                        := This action will display the Empire Report for this empire.
Dlg Empires 12 Name                                         := Send Message
Dlg Empires 12 Descr                                        := The Send Message action will display the Communicate window so that you can send a new message to this empire.
Dlg Empires 13 Name                                         := Send To News
Dlg Empires 13 Descr                                        := The Send To News action will display the Communicate window so that you can send a message to the Galactic News service.
Dlg Empires 14 Name                                         := Alliance Chambers
Dlg Empires 14 Descr                                        := If you current belong to an Alliance, this button will be enabled. Pressing it will display the Alliance Chambers window.
Dlg Empires 15 Name                                         := Comparisons
Dlg Empires 15 Descr                                        := This action will display the Comparisons window so that you can compare and view statistics on all of the empires.
Dlg Empires 16 Name                                         := Our Empire Report
Dlg Empires 16 Descr                                        := This action will display the Empire Report for our empire.
Dlg Empires 17 Name                                         := Close
Dlg Empires 17 Descr                                        := Closes this window.
Dlg Empire Options 1 Name                                   := Empire Options
Dlg Empire Options 1 Descr                                  := The Empire Options window displays statistics for your empire, and allows you to set specific options for your empire.
Dlg Empire Options 2 Name                                   := Summary Pane
Dlg Empire Options 2 Descr                                  := The Summary Pane displays summary information for your empire. Your empire flag is displayed along with your empire name and emperor name. Below that are displayed the total number of fleets in your empire, total ships, total bases, and total units in space. At the bottom are displayed the number of solar systems which contain your colonies, the number of your colonies, the total population in millions, and the number of races in your empire.
Dlg Empire Options 3 Name                                   := Options List
Dlg Empire Options 3 Descr                                  := The Options List displays a list of categories for you to choose from. The options are in categories of Statistics, Empire Options, Repair Priorities, Ministers, and Strategies. Selecting an option will display details on that option in the Details pane.

Dlg Empire Options 20 Name                                  := Total In Storage

Dlg Empire Options 37 Name                                  := Simultaneous Transit
Dlg Empire Options 37 Descr                                 := If this is set TRUE, then your ships will attempt to transit the warp point at the same time. Doing this raises the risk of the ships hitting each other and being destroyed. If this is set to FALSE, then ships will transit in order one at a time.
