Dlg Fleet Transfer 2 Descr                                  := This list displays all of the vehicles in the currently selected sector.
Dlg Fleet Transfer 3 Name                                   := Fleets In Sector List
Dlg Fleet Transfer 3 Descr                                  := This list displays all of the fleets that are present in the currently selected sector. Each fleet displays it flag, its name, its attack and defense formation, and a list of the task forces that make it up. Each task force displays its name, its attack and defense formation, its attack and defense strategy, and then a list of all of the vehicles that are within that task force.

Dlg Game Setup - Map 1 Name                                 := Game Setup – Map
Dlg Game Setup - Map 1 Descr                                := The Game Setup – Map window allows you to configure the physical makeup of the quadrant that you will play your game in.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 2 Name                                 := Quadrant Map
Dlg Game Setup - Map 2 Descr                                := The quadrant map displays the current layout of the quadrant you are playing in. This will normally start blank, and the map will not be determined until you start your game. If you decide to use the “Generate Map” action, then the quadrant map will be displayed.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 3 Name                                 := Quadrant Type
Dlg Game Setup - Map 3 Descr                                := This list allows you to select the type of Quadrant that you want to play in.

Dlg Game Setup - Map 4 Descr                                := General options that the map must obey.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 5 Name                                 := Quadrant Size
Dlg Game Setup - Map 5 Descr                                := The size of the quadrant you wish to play in. Small equates to 10-20 solar system, Medium equates to 30-60 solar systems, and large will result in 60-100 solar systems.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 6 Name                                 := All Warp Points Connected
Dlg Game Setup - Map 6 Descr                                := All solar systems in the quadrant must be connected via warp points. This means that you can reach all solar systems via travel through warp points. If this option is turned off, there will be portions of the quadrant you will not be able to reach until you develop the technology to open warp points.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 7 Name                                 := No Warp Points
Dlg Game Setup - Map 7 Descr                                := If this option is selected, then there will be no warp points present in the quadrant. You will not be able to travel to any other solar systems until you develop the technology to open warp points.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 8 Name                                 := Warp Points located anywhere in the system
Dlg Game Setup - Map 8 Descr                                := If this option is selected, then warp points can be located anywhere in the solar system. Normally, with this option off, warp points only show up in the outer reaches of the solar system.
Dlg Game Setup - Map 9 Name                                 := Finite Resources
Dlg Game Setup - Map 9 Descr                                := With this option off, all resources from a planet are infinite, meaning that they will never expire for the entire game. If this option is on, then resources of a planet are finite, and they will eventually run out.

Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 1 Name                         := Game Setup – Multiplayer
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 1 Descr                        := The Game Setup – Multiplayer window allows you to configure multiplayer options for this game.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 2 Name                         := Game Master Password
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 2 Descr                        := This edit box allows you to enter a game master password for the game. This password can be used to change players in the game.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 3 Name                         := Multiplayer Savegame Filename
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 3 Descr                        := This edit box allows you to enter a filename for the multiplayer game. This is the name of the game that is saved.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 4 Name                         := Savegame Directory Path
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 4 Descr                        := This edit box allows you to enter a path to save the game on. If you want the game saved in the standard savegame directory, then leave this blank. If you want the game saved in a different location, enter a path here.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 5 Name                         := Multiplayer Settings
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 5 Descr                        := This is a list of the options used for a multiplayer game.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 6 Name                         := Turn Style
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 6 Descr                        := The type of style used for turns in the game.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 7 Name                         := Turn Based Movement
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 7 Descr                        := Turns are taken in order, first player 1, then player 2, and so on. Each player moves all of their vehicles on their turn.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 8 Name                         := Simultaneous Movement
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 8 Descr                        := Turns are taken simultaneously by all players. Each player takes their turn and gives orders to their vehicles. Vehicle movement happens at the end of all player’s turns.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 9 Name                         := Play Style
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 9 Descr                        := Where the game is played.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 10 Name                        := Hot Seat
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 10 Descr                       := All players play the game on the same computer, and switch seats for each player’s turn.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 11 Name                        := Different Machines
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 11 Descr                       := Players are playing the game on different computers.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 12 Name                        := Connection Type
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 12 Descr                       := The way that the players are connected.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 13 Name                        := Manual File Moving
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 13 Descr                       := The savegame file is moved manually by players. This selection should be used if you plan to play by email or over the web.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 14 Name                        := Host
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 14 Descr                       := This player wishes to host the game. They will be responsible to collecting the player order files and generating the new savegame.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 15 Name                        := Player
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 15 Descr                       := This player will be a player in a hosted game. They will merely load the game and play their turn.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 16 Name                        := Provider Type
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 16 Descr                       := The method by which game files are moved between players.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 17 Name                        := Serial Connection
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 17 Descr                       := Two players are connected by a serial connection (a cable) between their two computers.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 18 Name                        := Modem Connection
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 18 Descr                       := Two players are connected over a modem connection.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 19 Name                        := IPX Connection
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 19 Descr                       := Multiple players are connected over a LAN.
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 20 Name                        := Internet TCP/IP
Dlg Game Setup – Multiplayer 20 Descr                       := Multiple players are connected over the Internet.

Dlg Game Setup - Victory Conditions 1 Descr                 := The Game Setup – Victory Conditions window is used to set the conditions under which the game will end.
Dlg Game Setup - Victory Conditions 2 Name                  := Victory Conditions List
Dlg Game Setup - Victory Conditions 2 Descr                 := Select a condition from this list for how the game will end. Each condition lists the criteria under which the game will end. During the game, these conditions can be viewed in the Scores window.

Dlg Intelligence 1 Name                                     := Intelligence
Dlg Intelligence 1 Descr                                    := The Intelligence Window allows you to set intelligence spending for offense and defense.
Dlg Intelligence 2 Name                                     := Summary Pane
Dlg Intelligence 2 Descr                                    := The Summary Pane displays summary information about your intelligence spending. At the top of the window is displayed the number of intelligence points you have to spend this turn. Next the statistics of your successes and failures for intelligence actions are displayed. The third section displays how many enemy empires there are, the estimated intelligence expenditure they make each turn, and how much we believe is devoted against us. The final section lists how many ally empires there are, the estimated intelligence expenditure by them each turn, and how much we believe they are spending against us.
Dlg Intelligence 3 Name                                     := Defensive Spending
Dlg Intelligence 3 Descr                                    := This setting determines what percentage of your intelligence points are spent in defense against enemy intelligence operations. Shift + left or right clicking on the arrow buttons will move the slider in increments of 10%.
Dlg Intelligence 4 Name                                     := Empire List
Dlg Intelligence 4 Descr                                    := The Empire Lists displays all of the other empires that you know of.
Dlg Intelligence 5 Name                                     := Focus Area
Dlg Intelligence 5 Descr                                    := The focus area determines what type of intelligence action you wish to take against this empire. You can press the downwards arrow to display a list of focus areas to choose from.
Dlg Intelligence 6 Name                                     := Spending
Dlg Intelligence 6 Descr                                    := The percentage of your intelligence points you are spending in intelligence actions against other empires. You can use the plus and minus arrow buttons to change the spending percentage. Shift + right or left clicking on the arrow buttons will move the slider in increments of 10%. Your total defensive spending percentage plus offensive spending percentage against all other empires cannot exceed 100%. 
Dlg Intelligence 7 Name                                     := Total Percentage Allocated
Dlg Intelligence 7 Descr                                    := This is the sum of the Defensive Spending, plus the spending against for each empire. Your total defensive spending percentage plus offensive spending percentage against all other empires cannot exceed 100%.
Dlg Intelligence 8 Name                                     := Expand Map
Dlg Intelligence 8 Descr                                    := Expands the Quadrant Map so that it is larger to view.
Dlg Intelligence 9 Name                                     := All Empires
Dlg Intelligence 9 Descr                                    := This option causes all empires that you know of to be displayed in the Empire List.
Dlg Intelligence 10 Name                                    := Ally Empires
Dlg Intelligence 10 Descr                                   := This option causes only your ally empires to be displayed in the Empire List.
Dlg Intelligence 11 Name                                    := Enemy Empires
Dlg Intelligence 11 Descr                                   := This option causes only enemy empires to be displayed in the Empire List.
Dlg Intelligence 12 Name                                    := Intel In Progress
Dlg Intelligence 12 Descr                                   := This option causes only empires that you are currently spending intelligence points against to be displayed in the Empire List.
Dlg Intelligence 13 Name                                    := Close
Dlg Intelligence 13 Descr                                   := Closes this window and saves all of your changes.
Dlg Intelligence 14 Name                                    := Intelligence List
Dlg Intelligence 14 Descr                                   := The Empire Lists displays all of the other empires that you know of. The focus area determines what type of intelligence action you wish to take against that empire. You can press the downwards arrow to display a list of focus areas to choose from. The spending column indicates the percentage of your intelligence points you are spending in intelligence actions against this empire. You can use the plus and minus arrow buttons to change the spending percentage. Your total defensive spending percentage plus offensive spending percentage against all other empires cannot exceed 100%.

Dlg Launch/Recover Units 1 Name                             := Launch/Recover Units
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 1 Descr                            := The Launch / Recover Units window allows you to launch and recover units from space. You can launch units from ships and planets into space. You can also recover units from space into ships and planets. Double-clicking a particular unit will transfer that unit to the currently selected target on the other side of the window.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 2 Name                             := Units In Cargo List
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 2 Descr                            := Displays a list of all of the ships and planets present in the current sector. For each ship or planet, the units in cargo (that can be launched) are displayed under it. Each vehicle displays the amount of cargo space used out of the total amount available. Each cargo item displays its size taken in cargo space.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 3 Name                             := Units In Space List
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 3 Descr                            := Displays a list of the units that are present in space in the current sector. Each unit displays the size in cargo space that it will take up.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 4 Name                             := Launch Unit
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 4 Descr                            := This action will launch the currently selected cargo item into space.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 5 Name                             := Amount
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 5 Descr                            := This selection displays how many items you wish to launch or recover at a time. Use the arrow keys to increase or decrease the amount. You can also click on the number and type in a specific amount.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 6 Name                             := Recover Unit
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 6 Descr                            := This action will recover the currently selected unit in the Units In Space List into the currently selected vehicle in the Units In Cargo List. The unit will only be recovered if there is sufficient cargo space remaining.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 7 Name                             := Close
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 7 Descr                            := Closes this window.
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 8 Name                             := Plus Button
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 8 Descr                            := Increase the Amount To Add by a factor of 10. 
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 9 Name                             := Minus Button
Dlg Launch/Recover Units 9 Descr                            := Decrease the Amount To Add by a factor of 10.

Dlg Log 1 Name                                              := Log
Dlg Log 1 Descr                                             := The Log Window displays all of the log messages for your empire. Log messages are informational notes generated by events or communications which take place. For example, when you construct a ship, a log message will be displayed informing you that this action took place last turn. If a communication is received from or sent to another empire, it will be displayed here. Think of the Log Window as your central news location.
Dlg Log 2 Name                                              := Summary Pane
Dlg Log 2 Descr                                             := The Summary Pane displays summary information about your Log messages. The current game date is displayed, then how many of the different log messages you have. At the bottom of the window are a breakdown of the different types of log messages for the currently selected category.
Dlg Log 3 Name                                              := Log List
Dlg Log 3 Descr                                             := The Log List displays all of the log messages that meet your currently selected filter criteria. Each message shows a picture, a subject of the message, the date the message was created, and a description for the message. When you move your mouse pointer over a picture, you will see a zoom icon. Clicking on the picture will display a larger version of the picture for you to view.  Clicking on the Event Portrait header will allow you to cycle through different display sizes for the list of log items.  Double-clicking on an event that references a particular system or planet will take you to that location in the system view. When you initially view the log each new turn, new items will be displayed with a grey background. After the initial view, each item is displayed with a black background.
Dlg Log 4 Name                                              := Expand Map
Dlg Log 4 Descr                                             := Expands the quadrant map to a larger size.
Dlg Log 5 Name                                              := Galactic News
Dlg Log 5 Descr                                             := Filters the Log List so that only Galactic News items are displayed. Galactic News is generated for global events and can be viewed by all players.
Dlg Log 6 Name                                              := Empire News
Dlg Log 6 Descr                                             := Filters the Log List so that only Empire News items are displayed. Empire News items are status messages caused by events that occur in your empire.
Dlg Log 7 Name                                              := Communications
Dlg Log 7 Descr                                             := Filters the Log List so that only Communications items are displayed. Communications items are messages from other empires to you.
Dlg Log 8 Name                                              := History
Dlg Log 8 Descr                                             := Filters the Log List so that only History items are displayed. History items are old log messages from previous turns.
Dlg Log 9 Name                                              := Sub Criteria
Dlg Log 9 Descr                                             := Depending on the Category you select, sub criteria options will be displayed here. These allow you to further filter the log list to log items on specific topics.
Dlg Log 10 Name                                             := Add Personal Note
Dlg Log 10 Descr                                            := The Add Personal Note button allows you to create a new log message in your log with text that you enter.
Dlg Log 11 Name                                             := Goto
Dlg Log 11 Descr                                            := Pressing this button will take you to the specific solar system and sector where the currently selected log message took place.
Dlg Log 12 Name                                             := Close
Dlg Log 12 Descr                                            := Closes this window.
Dlg Login 1 Name                                            := Login
Dlg Login 1 Descr                                           := The Login window is displayed to allow a player to login to a multiplayer game. In Simultaneous Games, players can play their turns in any order. When the game is loaded, the Login window is displayed to indicate which player is about to take their turn.
Dlg Login 2 Name                                            := Empire List
Dlg Login 2 Descr                                           := The Empire List displays all of the empires in the current game. Each empire is displayed with its flag and empire name.
Dlg Login 3 Name                                            := Password
Dlg Login 3 Descr                                           := The Password edit box is used to enter a password if one is set for this empire. You cannot login as a player unless your password is correct.
Dlg Login 4 Name                                            := Login
Dlg Login 4 Descr                                           := Starts the game for the currently selected empire if the password is correct.
Dlg Login 5 Name                                            := Cancel
Dlg Login 5 Descr                                           := Cancels the login and closes the window.

The display shows the solar system that you select in the Quadrant Map (in the bottom left of the window). See the section Main Window – System Display for more details.

Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 1 Name                         := Main Window  - Ship List
Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 1 Descr                        := The Main Window – Ship List displays all of the objects in the currently selected sector on the Main Window – System Display. You can use this list to get reports on objects, or to select them for giving orders to.
Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 2 Name                         := Ship List
Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 2 Descr                        := Each object will be displayed with its picture and name, and if it’s owned by a player, with the owner’s empire flag. In addition, if you own the vehicle some additional information may be displayed. For ships that you own, three bars will be displayed indicating the damage, supplies, and ordnance remaining on the ship. Also the movement remaining out of the total movement will be displayed at the bottom of the square.
Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 3 Name                         := The list can display in one of two modes. If there are multiple objects present, then a list of those objects will be displayed. However, if there is only one object, then just the header of that object’s report will be displayed. In the list mode if you right-click on an item, then you will display just that item in the list. If only the one item is displayed, then right-clicking on the item will display the full report for that object.
Dlg Main Window  - Ship List 3 Descr                        := If only one object is displayed, then any orders you give in the Main Window – Orders Panel will be for just that object. If there are a list of objects displayed, you can left-click on them to highlight them, and then orders given will be for all selected objects.

Dlg Main Window  - System Display 1 Name                    := Main Window  - System Display
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 1 Descr                   := The Main Window – System Display is where you can interact with the solar system and give your vehicles orders.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 2 Name                    := System Display
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 2 Descr                   := The Main Display shows your current viewpoint on the solar system. The display shows the solar system that you select in the Quadrant Map (in the bottom left of the window). Each solar system is comprised of a hexagon grid which represents each of the individual sectors in the solar system. Each sector can contain multiple objects.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 3 Name                    := Left-click
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 3 Descr                   := Left-clicking on a hex (sector) selects that hex and it will be surrounded by a double white line. The Ship List will display all of the objects that are in that sector.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 4 Name                    := Right-click
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 4 Descr                   := Right-clicking displays a menu of actions that you can take at this location. See the Orders Menu below for more details.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 5 Name                    := Mouse pointer on the edge of the window
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 5 Descr                   := Moving your mouse pointer to the left or fight edge of the screen will rotate your viewpoint around the solar system. If you move your mouse pointer to the top or bottom of the screen, your viewpoint will move forward or backwards over the solar system.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 6 Name                    := Scroll Wheel
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 6 Descr                   := Scrolling on the scroll wheel of your mouse will raise or lower your viewpoint above the plane of the solar system.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 7 Name                    := Hex Grid
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 7 Descr                   := Each hex in a solar system indicates one sector. It requires 1 movement point to move through 1 sector. So a ship with 5 movement points could move through 5 hexes in a single turn. You may notice that some hexes are colored differently. The color of the hex indicates what your current sight level is for that hex. Each ship with sensors has a sight range. As they move through a solar system, they will “see” all sectors in that range around them. For you to determine what objects are present in a solar system, you need to send ships to scan (See) all of the sectors within them. The colors for hexes correspond to:
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 8 Name                    := Light Red – You cannot currently see this sector and have never seen this sector in the past.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 8 Descr                   := Dark Red – This sector is blocked and you cannot move through it.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 9 Name                    := Gray – You cannot currently see this sector but you have seen it in the past.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 9 Descr                   := Green – You can currently see what is in this sector.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 10 Name                   := Blue – Your mouse pointer is over this sector.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 10 Descr                  := White – This is the currently selected sector.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 11 Name                   := System Modifiers
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 11 Descr                  := System modifiers are modifiers which apply to the entire solar system. They are a helpful list of items which effect over a wide area. For example, in the last to the left, the System Modifiers indicate that supply and ordnance will be distributed across the entire solar system. It also indicates that all colonies generating resources will have them automatically added to your empire’s treasury at the end of the turn.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 12 Name                   := Colonization Icons
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 12 Descr                  := Colonization Icons are displayed to indicated whether your empire can colonize a given planet. If there is no icon present, then you cannot colonize the planet at all. If a red icon is displayed, then you can colonize the planet, but your race cannot breathe the atmosphere. If a colony is established here, then it will be “Domed” which means that it will have a much smaller amount of space for facilities, population, and cargo. A green icon indicates that you can colonize this planet, and that your race can breathe the atmosphere. This is the best type of planet to colonize. As your technology develops, you may gain the ability to colonize additional planet types. If the planet already has a colony, then the icon will not be displayed.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 13 Name                   := Planet Ownership Flag
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 13 Descr                  := This flag is displayed over any sector where a colonized planet is present. The top of the flag is a rectangle containing the flag for the owner of the colony. Underneath it are 3 numbers and a colored bar indicating how many bases, ships, and units are present in the sector (that are owned by this player, and that you can currently see), and the bar indicates how much population is present (out of the maximum the planet can hold).
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 14 Name                   := Vehicle Ownership Flag
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 14 Descr                  := This flag is displayed over any sector where there are vehicles present be they ships, bases, or units. The top of the flag is a triangle containing the flag for the owner of the vehicles. Underneath it are 3 numbers indicating how many bases, ships, and units are present in the sector (that are owned by this player, and that you can currently see).
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 15 Name                   := Orders Menu
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 15 Descr                  := The Orders Menu is displayed when you right click on a sector in the System Display. The Orders Menu is composed of several sections:
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 16 Name                   := Orders – These are orders that you can give to the vehicles selected in the Ships List. If no vehicles are selected, then there will be very few orders to pick from.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 16 Descr                  := Reports – These are reports that you can get on objects located in this sector.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 17 Name                   := Selections – These are objects that you can select in the Ship List.
Dlg Main Window  - System Display 17 Descr                  := 
Dlg Planets 1 Name                                          := Planets
Dlg Planets 1 Descr                                         := The Planets Window is where you can get a summary view of all of the planets you have discovered throughout the quadrant. This is a good place to find the best planets to colonize and to send colony ships to colonize them.
Dlg Planets 2 Name                                          := Summary Pane
Dlg Planets 2 Descr                                         := The Summary Pane displays statistics on all of the planets you have discovered. Statistics displayed are Known Systems (the number of solar systems you have discovered in the quadrant), Number Of Planets (the number of planets you have discovered in the quadrant), Number Of Colonizable Planets (the total number of planets that you know of that you can colonize at your current technology level), Planets which are owned by Enemies, Planets which are owned by Allies, Planets which are owned by Non-Aligned (not allies or enemies), Planets which are not Colonized, Planets which are breathable (breathable and colonizable), Colonizing Ships (the number of colony ships you have), and Available Colonizing Ships (the number of colony ships you have that don’t already have colonize orders).
Dlg Planets 3 Name                                          := Quadrant Map
Dlg Planets 3 Descr                                         := The Quadrant Map displays all of the solar systems in the quadrant that you have discovered. When you move your mouse pointer over a planet in the list, the solar system that planet resides in will be highlighted in the quadrant map.
Dlg Planets 4 Name                                          := Planet List
Dlg Planets 4 Descr                                         := The Planet lists displays all planets that meet the current Filter settings you have defined. Each planets is displayed with the columns you have selected under Layout. You can left click a row to select that row. You can also right-click a row to display a detailed report for that planet. Double-clicking on a particular planet will take you to that planet on the system view.
Dlg Planets 5 Name                                          := Expand Map
Dlg Planets 5 Descr                                         := Pressing this button will expand the quadrant map so that it is larger.
Dlg Planets 6 Name                                          := Layout
Dlg Planets 6 Descr                                         := The layout button will let you select from a list of layouts. Each layout displays a different set of columns which provide different information about each planet. This action also allows you to create, edit and delete custom layouts where you choose which columns of data will be shown.
Dlg Planets 7 Name                                          := Physical Statistics
Dlg Planets 7 Descr                                         := Displays the columns Picture, Name, Coordinates, Planet Type, Planet Size, and Planet Atmosphere.
Dlg Planets 8 Name                                          := Conditions
Dlg Planets 8 Descr                                         := Displays the columns Picture, Name, Coordinates, Planet Conditions, Radiation, Gravity, and Temperature.
Dlg Planets 9 Name                                          := Value
Dlg Planets 9 Descr                                         := Displays the columns Picture, Name, Coordinates, Mineral Value, Organics Value, and Radioactives Value.
Dlg Planets 10 Name                                         := Colony Owner
Dlg Planets 10 Descr                                        := Displays the columns Picture, Name, Coordinates, Colony Owner, and Population.
Dlg Planets 11 Name                                         := Ship Enroute
Dlg Planets 11 Descr                                        := Displays the columns Picture, Name, Coordinates, Ship Name, Ship Location, and Arrival Time.
Dlg Planets 12 Name                                         := Filter
Dlg Planets 12 Descr                                        := The Filter button will let you select from a list of filters. The filter defines what planets will actually be displayed in the list.
Dlg Planets 13 Name                                         := All
Dlg Planets 13 Descr                                        := All planets that you have ever seen will be displayed.

Dlg Planets 14 Descr                                        := All planets that have colonies will be displayed.

Dlg Planets 21 Name                                         := Ship Enroute

Dlg Planets 22 Name                                         := Asteroids
Dlg Planets 22 Descr                                        := All asteroids that you have ever seen will be displayed.
Dlg Planets 23 Name                                         := Special
Dlg Planets 23 Descr                                        := All planets that have ruins on them will be displayed.
Dlg Planets 24 Name                                         := Send Colonizer
Dlg Planets 24 Descr                                        := This command will send the nearest available colony ship you own to colonize the currently selected planet. Any colony ship that already has orders will be ignored.
Dlg Planets 25 Name                                         := Goto
Dlg Planets 25 Descr                                        := Pressing this button will close the window and take you to the location of the currently selected planet in the list.
Dlg Planets 26 Name                                         := Close
Dlg Planets 26 Descr                                        := Closes this window.

Dlg Planets 27 Descr                                        := The number of solar systems in the quadrant that you have discovered or know of.

Dlg Planets 29 Descr                                        := The total number of colonizable planets that you have seen throughout the quadrant.
Dlg Planets 30 Name                                         := Planets which are owned by Enemies
Dlg Planets 30 Descr                                        := The total number of planets which are owned by enemy empires.
Dlg Planets 31 Name                                         := Planets which are owned by Allies

Dlg Planets 32 Name                                         := Planets which are owned by Non-Aligned
Dlg Planets 32 Descr                                        := The total number of planets which are owned by empires that are not our enemy or ally.
Dlg Planets 33 Name                                         := Planets which are not Colonized

Dlg Planets 34 Name                                         := Planets which are Breathable

Dlg Players 1 Name                                          := Players
Dlg Players 1 Descr                                         := The Players Window allows you to change whether players are under computer control or not.
Dlg Players 2 Name                                          := Empire List
Dlg Players 2 Descr                                         := The Empire List displays all of the empires present in the game. If the selection box is checked, then that empire is under computer control. You can change the selections by clicking on the box. Any empire which does not have a check in front of it will be under human player control from then on.

Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 1 Name                     := Player Setup – Racial Traits
Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 1 Descr                    := The Player Setup – Racial Traits window allows you to select the racial traits for the race which runs this empire.
Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 2 Name                     := Racial Points Available
Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 2 Descr                    := This section displays how many racial points are available for you to spend on your empire. As Racial Traits are selected, the cost of each racial trait is subtracted from your points available. You cannot finish creating your empire unless the Racial Points Available are greater than or equal to zero.
Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 3 Name                     := Racial Traits List
Dlg Player Setup – Racial Traits 3 Descr                    := The Racial Traits list displays all of the racial traits available for a race. You can select multiple items for your race and its corresponding cost will be deducted from the Racial Point Available. Each Racial Trait is listed with its name, cost, and the bonuses it will give to your empire.
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 1 Name                        := Player Setup – Technology
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 1 Descr                       := The Player Setup – Technology window allows you to select the starting technology that your empire has discovered.
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 2 Name                        := Research Points Available
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 2 Descr                       := This section displays how many research points are available for you to spend on your empire. If the points are greater than zero, then you can add technology levels to your empire. You cannot create your empire unless the Research Points Available are greater than or equal to zero.
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 3 Name                        := Technology Chart
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 3 Descr                       := The Technology Chart section displays the icon, name, and description for the current research area that your mouse pointer is over.
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 4 Name                        := Research Area List
Dlg Player Setup – Technology 4 Descr                       := The Research Area List displays all of the research areas that your Empire can discover. Each research area displays its icon, name, cost for the next level, and your empire’s current level in that area. By pressing the plus and minus buttons you can increase or decrease your empire’s current level in this research area. When you increase a technology level you will deduct the cost of the level from the Research Points Available. By adding technology levels you may gain access to new research areas that are not currently present in the list. In addition, some research areas are only available if your race has certain racial traits.
Dlg Player Setup – History 1 Name                           := Player Setup – History
Dlg Player Setup – History 1 Descr                          := The Player Setup – History window allows you to enter background descriptions for your empire.

Dlg Player Setup – History 2 Descr                          := This edit box allows you to enter a detailed description about the biology of your race.

Dlg Player Setup – History 3 Descr                          := This edit box allows you to enter a detailed description about the society of your empire.
Dlg Player Setup – History 4 Name                           := History
Dlg Player Setup – History 4 Descr                          := This edit box allows you to enter a detailed description about the history of your empire.
Dlg Quadrant Map 1 Name                                     := Quadrant Map
Dlg Quadrant Map 1 Descr                                    := The Quadrant Map is an enlarged version of the Main Window – Quadrant Map. It displays all of the solar systems that have been discovered by your empire in the galaxy. Each solar system is depicted with an empty circle (you have a presence in the solar system), a solid circle (you have no presence in the solar system) or a solid cross (you and an enemy both have a presence in the solar system).
Dlg Quadrant Map 2 Name                                     := Quadrant Map
Dlg Quadrant Map 2 Descr                                    := The quadrant map is composed of two types of items - solar systems and warp points. Solar systems are represented by asterisk like icons. Warp point connections are represented by lines between the solar system icons. If a solar system is represented with a circle, it indicates that the solar system has visible empires present within it (even your own). If the solar system has a square around it, then that is the currently selected solar system and is displayed in the Main Window – System Display. If you move your mouse pointer over a solar system icon, the name for that solar system will be displayed on the map.
Dlg Quick Start 1 Name                                      := Quick Start
Dlg Quick Start 1 Descr                                     := The Quick Start window allows you to pick an empire for use in a quick start game. A quick start game begins the game with all of the default settings and a single human player.
Dlg Quick Start 2 Name                                      := Empires List
Dlg Quick Start 2 Descr                                     := The Empires List displays all of the empires present for you to choose from in the game. Select one to have its details displayed in the Empires Details section.
Dlg Quick Start 3 Name                                      := Empire Details
Dlg Quick Start 3 Descr                                     := The Empire Details section displays specific details about the empire selected in the Empires List. The Empire Details panel shows the race portrait, the empire name, the empire flag, the home planet type, the home atmosphere type, and the ship style for this empire. A brief description for this empire is displayed at the bottom of the panel.
Dlg Quick Start 4 Name                                      := Begin
Dlg Quick Start 4 Descr                                     := Begins the game with the selected empire in the Empires List.
Dlg Quick Start 5 Name                                      := Cancel
Dlg Quick Start 5 Descr                                     := Cancels the game and closes the window.
Dlg Queue Settings 1 Name                                   := Queue Settings
Dlg Queue Settings 1 Descr                                  := The Construction Queue Settings window allows you to set settings for the current construction queue.
Dlg Queue Settings 2 Name                                   := Settings List
Dlg Queue Settings 2 Descr                                  := There are three options you can select for any construction queue.
Dlg Queue Settings 3 Name                                   := On Hold
Dlg Queue Settings 3 Descr                                  := This sets the construction queue on hold meaning that all construction is paused. When you turn this setting off, the constructions will start up right where they left off.
Dlg Queue Settings 4 Name                                   := Emergency Build
Dlg Queue Settings 4 Descr                                  := Emergency Build allows your construction queue to build at 150% of its normal rate for up to ten turns. At the end of ten turns, or when you turn this setting off, the queue will be in Slow Build for as many turns as it was in Emergency Build. In Slow Build mode, the construction queue will build at 25% of its normal rate.
Dlg Queue Settings 5 Name                                   := Repeat Build
Dlg Queue Settings 5 Descr                                  := Repeat build indicates that the construction queue should build what’s currently in its list endlessly. Items will not be removed from the list as they are completed, but the queue will move from one item to the next and then start again at the top when it reaches the bottom.
Dlg Queue Settings 6 Name                                   := Close
Dlg Queue Settings 6 Descr                                  := Closes this window and saves any changes that you have made.

Dlg Report - Asteroids 6 Descr                              := The resource value of this asteroid group.

Dlg Report - Asteroids 7 Descr                              := A general description for these asteroids.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 1 Name                     := Report - Combat Piece Ground
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 1 Descr                    := The Report – Combat Piece Ground displays a complete status report on a vehicle in ground combat.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 2 Name                     := Portrait
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 2 Descr                    := A portrait of the vehicle. You can click on the portrait to get an enlarged version of it.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 3 Name                     := Class
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 3 Descr                    := The name of the vehicle design that this vehicle is based on.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 4 Name                     := Size
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 4 Descr                    := The name of the vehicle size that this vehicle is based on.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 5 Name                     := Heading
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 5 Descr                    := The current angle heading of this vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 6 Name                     := Speed
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 6 Descr                    := The current speed at which this vehicle is moving.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 7 Name                     := Shields
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 7 Descr                    := The current number of shield points and the maximum number of shield points that this vehicle maintains. Once a vehicle’s shields reach zero, damage will next hit the armor of the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 8 Name                     := Armor
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 8 Descr                    := The current tonnage of armor and the maximum tonnage of armor that this vehicle maintains. Once a vehicle’s armor reaches zero, damage will next hit the internal components of the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 9 Name                     := Structure
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 9 Descr                    := The current tonnage of internal structure (all components on the vehicle) and the maximum tonnage of internal structure that this vehicle maintains. Damage is applied first against components located in the outer structure and then components located in the inner structure. Once a vehicle’s structure reaches zero, the vehicle is destroyed.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 10 Name                    := Supplies
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 10 Descr                   := The current amount of supplies and the maximum amount of supplies this vehicle contains. Once a vehicle’s supplies reach zero, it can no longer move or fire energy weapons.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 11 Name                    := Ordnance
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 11 Descr                   := The current amount of ordnance and the maximum amount of ordnance this vehicle contains. Once a vehicle’s ordnance reaches zero, it can no longer fire weapons which require ordnance.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 12 Name                    := Crew
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 12 Descr                   := The current amount of crew and the maximum amount of crew this vehicle contains.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 13 Name                    := Damage Tab
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 13 Descr                   := The Damage Tab displays the overall internal damage amounts this vehicle has received.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 14 Name                    := Ship Layout
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 14 Descr                   := The ship layout is a smaller version of the vehicle layout you created in the Create Design window. It displays all of the components that are on the vehicle, and shows the damage percent that each component has sustained. The damage percent goes from 0% (no damage) in green, to 100% (completely damaged) in red. A component which is damaged may no longer work.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 15 Name                    := Damage Statistics
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 15 Descr                   := The damage statistics displays the percentage damage to the different component types on the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 16 Name                    := Deck Buttons
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 16 Descr                   := The deck buttons allow you to see the components on the different decks of the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 17 Name                    := Targeting Tab
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 17 Descr                   := The Targeting Tab displays a list of your current weapon’s targets.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 18 Name                    := Targeting List
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 18 Descr                   := The Targeting List displays each of the weapons on your vehicle and what enemy vehicle they are currently targeted on. Each line shows a picture of the weapon, the name of the weapon, the time remaining till the weapon reloads, the total time required to reload the weapon, the maximum range of the weapon, the name of the target it is targeted on, the percent of damage on the enemy vehicle, and the distance from this vehicle to the enemy vehicle. You can right-click on a weapon to get a report on that weapon.

Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 19 Descr                   := The Cargo Tab displays a list of all of the cargo carried by the vehicle.

Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 20 Descr                   := The Cargo List displays each of the cargo items on your vehicle. Each cargo item displays its picture and the amount of damage it has taken. You can right-click on a cargo item to get a report on that item.

Dlg Report - Combat Piece Ground 25 Descr                   := The Status List displays general status information about your vehicle such as its current Movement Orders, whether its using AutoTargeting , and whether its using AutoMove.

Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 1 Descr                     := The Report – Combat Piece Space displays a complete status report on a vehicle or planet in space combat.

Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 2 Descr                     := A portrait of the vehicle. You can click on the portrait to get an enlarged version of it.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 3 Name                      := Class
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 3 Descr                     := The name of the vehicle design that this vehicle is based on.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 4 Name                      := Size
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 4 Descr                     := The name of the vehicle size that this vehicle is based on.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 5 Name                      := Heading
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 5 Descr                     := The current angle heading of this vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 6 Name                      := Speed
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 6 Descr                     := The current speed at which this vehicle is moving.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 7 Name                      := Shields
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 7 Descr                     := The current number of shield points and the maximum number of shield points that this vehicle maintains. Once a vehicle’s shields reach zero, damage will next hit the armor of the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 8 Name                      := Armor
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 8 Descr                     := The current tonnage of armor and the maximum tonnage of armor that this vehicle maintains. Once a vehicle’s armor reaches zero, damage will next hit the internal components of the vehicle.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 9 Name                      := Structure
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 9 Descr                     := The current tonnage of internal structure (all components on the vehicle) and the maximum tonnage of internal structure that this vehicle maintains. Damage is applied first against components located in the outer structure and then components located in the inner structure. Once a vehicle’s structure reaches zero, the vehicle is destroyed.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 10 Name                     := Supplies
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 10 Descr                    := The current amount of supplies and the maximum amount of supplies this vehicle contains. Once a vehicle’s supplies reach zero, it can no longer move or fire energy weapons.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 11 Name                     := Ordnance
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 11 Descr                    := The current amount of ordnance and the maximum amount of ordnance this vehicle contains. Once a vehicle’s ordnance reaches zero, it can no longer fire weapons which require ordnance.
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 12 Name                     := Crew
Dlg Report - Combat Piece Space 12 Descr                    := The current amount of crew and the maximum amount of crew this vehicle contains.

Dlg Report - Damage Type 1 Name                             := Report - Damage Type
Dlg Report - Damage Type 1 Descr                            := A list of any requirements that are needed for this damage type to be used.
Dlg Report - Damage Type 2 Name                             := Name
Dlg Report - Damage Type 2 Descr                            := The name of this damage type.
Dlg Report - Damage Type 3 Name                             := Description
Dlg Report - Damage Type 3 Descr                            := A general text description for this damage type.
Dlg Report - Damage Type 4 Name                             := Penetration and Damage List
Dlg Report - Damage Type 4 Descr                            := A list of the penetration and damage percentages for this damage type. A damage type may have special capabilities against certain targets. If a penetration percent is listed, then this damage type penetrates that shield type, vehicle type, or armor type in a different way than normal. Normal damage does not penetrate anything, in other words it has a penetration percent of 0. If a damage type states that it has a penetration percent of 50%, then 50% of the damage will penetrate the defense automatically. If a damage type states that it has a damage percent of 200%, then this damage type will do twice the normal damage to this defense type.

Dlg Report - Damage Type 5 Descr                            := A list of the special abilities that this damage type has.
Dlg Report - Damage Type 6 Name                             := Requirements List

Dlg Report - Fleet 11 Descr                                 := This tab displays a list of all of the vehicles in this fleet.

Dlg Report - Fleet 12 Descr                                 := This list displays the ships that are in this fleet. Each box displays the picture of the ship, the name of the ship, the task force number this ship belongs to, and the group that this ship belongs within the task force. Dlg Report - Fleet 13 Name                                  := Task Forces Tab
Dlg Report - Fleet 13 Descr                                 := This tab displays the task forces that make up this fleet.
Dlg Report - Fleet 14 Name                                  := Task Force List
Dlg Report - Fleet 14 Descr                                 := The task force list displays a list of all of the task forces within this fleet. Task forces are grouping of ships within a fleet that have distinct strategies. Each task force displays its task force number, its name, the number of vehicles in the task force, the attack formation, the defense formation, the attack strategy, and the defense strategy. The formations and strategies have magnifying glass icons next to them. By clicking on these magnifying glass buttons, you can get a report on the formation or strategy.
Dlg Report - Fleet 15 Name                                  := Atk Form Tab
Dlg Report - Fleet 15 Descr                                 := This tab displays the attack formation for this fleet.
Dlg Report - Fleet 16 Name                                  := Formation Grid
Dlg Report - Fleet 16 Descr                                 := The formation grid displays the formation that this fleet will use when attacking. The grid displays the location of each task force within the fleet during combat.
Dlg Report - Fleet 17 Name                                  := Def Form Tab
Dlg Report - Fleet 17 Descr                                 := This tab displays the defense formation for this fleet.
Dlg Report - Fleet 18 Name                                  := Formation Grid
Dlg Report - Fleet 18 Descr                                 := The formation grid displays the formation that this fleet will use when defending. The grid displays the location of each task force within the fleet during combat.
Dlg Report - Fleet 19 Name                                  := WP Transit Tab
Dlg Report - Fleet 19 Descr                                 := This tab displays the order in which ships in this fleet will transit a warp point.
Dlg Report - Fleet 20 Name                                  := Transit List
Dlg Report - Fleet 20 Descr                                 := The Transit List displays a list of each of the ships in the fleet. Next to each ship is a number indicating the order in which the ships will transit through a warp point.
Dlg Report - Formation 1 Name                               := Report - Formation
Dlg Report - Formation 1 Descr                              := The formation grid displays the location of each object within the formation. There are two types of formations – Fleet and Task Force. For fleet formations, the grid elements will show the location of each task force. For task force formations, the grid elements will show four types of items. “L” represents the leader of the task force, “C” represents Core ships, “E” represents Escort ships, “P” represents Picket ships. The letters are followed by numbers indicating the nth vehicle in that group. All positions on the grid are relative to the Leader vehicle. All ships in the task force will attempt to maintain their position relative to the leader during combat.

Dlg Report - Planet 1 Name                                  := Report - Planet
Dlg Report - Planet 1 Descr                                 := The Report – Planet displays a complete status report on a planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 2 Name                                  := Portrait
Dlg Report - Planet 2 Descr                                 := A portrait of the planet. You can click on the portrait to get an enlarged version of it. The portrait box also includes a flag for the empire which has a colony on the planet and the name of the planet. The portrait also contains Status Icons that indicate special status for the colony on the planet. See the topic on Status Icons for a complete list of these and what they mean.
Dlg Report - Planet 3 Name                                  := Type
Dlg Report - Planet 3 Descr                                 := The type of this planet – Rock, Ice, or Gas.
Dlg Report - Planet 4 Name                                  := Size
Dlg Report - Planet 4 Descr                                 := The size of this planet. The larger the size of the planet, the more population, facilities and cargo that can be contained on it.
Dlg Report - Planet 5 Name                                  := Atmosphere
Dlg Report - Planet 5 Descr                                 := The atmosphere of the planet – None, Oxygen, Methane, Hydrogen, Carbon Dioxide. A colony that you place on the planet will be domed or not based on whether your race can breathe this atmosphere or not.
Dlg Report - Planet 6 Name                                  := Conditions
Dlg Report - Planet 6 Descr                                 := The physical conditions on the planet surface. This is a description of how difficult living on the surface will be. Conditions range from Optimal to Deadly. The better the conditions on the planet, the happier and reproductive your population will be. The worse the conditions on the planet, the higher the migration away from the planet will be by your population.
Dlg Report - Planet 7 Name                                  := Colony Type
Dlg Report - Planet 7 Descr                                 := The type of colony this is. This is a general description that you assign the colony when you colonize the planet. It helps you determine what purpose you want to use the colony for.
Dlg Report - Planet 8 Name                                  := Population
Dlg Report - Planet 8 Descr                                 := The amount of population on the planet. The population of the planet is in units of millions (M).
Dlg Report - Planet 9 Name                                  := Intel
Dlg Report - Planet 9 Descr                                 := The number of intelligence points that this colony is generating each turn. Intelligence points will only reach your empire if there is a Spaceport facility in the system.
Dlg Report - Planet 10 Name                                 := Research
Dlg Report - Planet 10 Descr                                := The number of research points that this colony is generating each turn. Research points will only reach your empire if there is a Spaceport facility in the system.
Dlg Report - Planet 11 Name                                 := Planet Value
Dlg Report - Planet 11 Descr                                := The resource value of this planet. If this is a finite resources game, then these values will be in kT of resources, indicating the number of resources of each type that remain on the planet. If this is a normal resource game, then the values for each resource will be in percentages. These percentages indicate the percentage of this type of resource that your facilities will generate. For example, if you have a Mineral Miner facility on the planet which produces 500 minerals per turn, and the planet has a value of 110% minerals, then your facility will actually generate 550 minerals per turn.
Dlg Report - Planet 12 Name                                 := Production (Net)
Dlg Report - Planet 12 Descr                                := The actual production in resources for this colony. This is the total amount of resources that this planet is generating minus the maintenance cost of your facilities.
Dlg Report - Planet 13 Name                                 := Surface Tab
Dlg Report - Planet 13 Descr                                := This tab displays information about the surface of the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 14 Name                                 := Radiation
Dlg Report - Planet 14 Descr                                := The radiation level on the surface of the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 15 Name                                 := Gravity
Dlg Report - Planet 15 Descr                                := The amount of gravity on the surface of the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 16 Name                                 := Temperature
Dlg Report - Planet 16 Descr                                := The average temperature on the surface of the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 17 Name                                 := Planetary Damage List
Dlg Report - Planet 17 Descr                                := A list of any specific damage that is present on the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 18 Name                                 := Occupying Troops On Planet List
Dlg Report - Planet 18 Descr                                := A list of any enemy troops which have landed on the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 19 Name                                 := Races Tab
Dlg Report - Planet 19 Descr                                := This tab displays information about the races on the planet.
Dlg Report - Planet 20 Name                                 := Races List
Dlg Report - Planet 20 Descr                                := The Races List displays all of the different races that inhabit this planet.  Each race displays its portrait, its name, the race population, the migration rate, the birth rate, the mood of the population, and the loyalty of the population. You can right click on an item to get a report on it.

Hull structure is the amount of damage that this design can withstand before it is destroyed. Each 1 point of damage will destroy 1 kT of hull structure.

Dlg Report - Vehicle Design 12 Descr                        := The number of movement points that this vehicle will get each turn. There are actually two types of movement points – space and ground. Dlg Research 1 Name                                         := Research
Dlg Research 1 Descr                                        := The Research Window is used to control your empire’s research of new technologies. As your empire generates research points, you spend the points in this window to develop new technologies.
Dlg Research 2 Name                                         := Research Points Available
Dlg Research 2 Descr                                        := The number of research points that your empire currently generates each turn. Research points are generated by Research Center facilities on your colonies.

Dlg Research 3 Descr                                        := When your cursor is hovering over a research area in the list below, this area displays the picture, name and text description of the research area.

Dlg Research 4 Descr                                        := This bar displays your current percent spending on the selected research area. This can range from 0 to 100 percent.
Dlg Research 5 Name                                         := Progress
Dlg Research 5 Descr                                        := This bar displays your progress in researching this research area. When the progress is full then you will achieve the next technology level in the selected area. The estimated time to completion is also displayed in years (0.1 years equals one turn).
Dlg Research 6 Name                                         := Expected Results
Dlg Research 6 Descr                                        := The expected results displays a list of the different items you can expect to receive if you achieve the next technology level in this research area.
Dlg Research 7 Name                                         := Research List
Dlg Research 7 Descr                                        := The research list displays all of the research areas that you currently know of. More areas will become available as you gain technology and discover them. Each item in the list displays a picture and a name for the research area. Current level is your current level in this technology area. Cost is the cost in research points to achieve the next level in this technology area. Progress displays a bar indicating how close you are to achieving the next level. Spending displays your current percentage spending on this research area. You can click on the arrows or the bar to increase and decrease the percentage of spending. You can only increase your spending percent to use up the remaining percent available. The total spending percentage can only be 100%.
Dlg Research 8 Name                                         := Total Percentage Allocated
Dlg Research 8 Descr                                        := The total of all of the individual research area spending. This amount cannot exceed 100%.

Dlg Research 13 Descr                                       := This selection displays only the Weapon Technology research areas in the research list.

Dlg Retrofit 1 Name                                         := Retrofit
Dlg Retrofit 1 Descr                                        := The Retrofit window allows you to choose a design to retrofit your current ship to.
Dlg Retrofit 2 Name                                         := Design List
Dlg Retrofit 2 Descr                                        := The designs list displays all of the designs that your ship can be retrofitted to. Only designs of the same size can be used, and the list will not show the design currently being used. The cost displayed is the cost to retrofit to the new design. The cost is calculated based on the difference in components between your current design and the design in the list. You can right click an item in the list to display the design report for that item.

Dlg Ships 1 Name                                            := Ships
Dlg Ships 1 Descr                                           := The Ships Window displays all of your ships, fleets, and unit groups throughout your empire.
Dlg Ships 2 Name                                            := Ships Statistics
Dlg Ships 2 Descr                                           := The ship statistics displays summary information about the ships in your empire. The “Ships / Mothballed” item displays how many total ships you have and how many ships are mothballed. The “Bases / Mothballed” item displays how many bases you have and how many bases are mothballed. The “Units In Space” item displays the total number of units you have in space (units you have in unit groups). “Fleets” displays the total number of fleets you own. “Research Points Produced” displays the total amount of research points that your empire produces. “Intelligence Points Produced” displays the total amount of intelligence points that your empire produces. “Total Resources Produced” displays the total amount of resources that your empire produces. “Maintenance Cost” displays the total maintenance cost in resources that your empire must pay each turn to maintain your vehicles and colonies.

If you click on the header of the picture column, it will change the size of the picture and also the height of each row and allow more rows to be displayed on each screen.

Dlg TCPIP Host 1 Name                                       := TCP/IP Host
Dlg TCPIP Host 1 Descr                                      := The TCP/IP Host window allows a player to host a simultaneous turn game over the Internet, LAN, or modem. The host determines which players get to join the game, and processes the turn when all players have completed their orders.
Dlg TCPIP Host 2 Name                                       := Game Date
Dlg TCPIP Host 2 Descr                                      := The current date of the game turn. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 3 Name                                       := Host Location
Dlg TCPIP Host 3 Descr                                      := The IP address location of the host. This defaults to the current IP address for this machine, but it can be changed by using the “Select IP Address” button. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 4 Name                                       := Status
Dlg TCPIP Host 4 Descr                                      := The current status of the game. This will indicate when a turn needs to be processed, when the host is waiting for players to take their turns, etc. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 5 Name                                       := Empire List (Player List)
Dlg TCPIP Host 5 Descr                                      := A list of all of the empires in the game. This includes both human controlled empires and compute controlled empires. The list displays the empire flag, empire name, player name, email address, and status of each player (whether they have submitted a turn or not). 
Dlg TCPIP Host 6 Name                                       := Chat Messages List
Dlg TCPIP Host 6 Descr                                      := This list displays all of the chat messages sent by each player. All players and the host can see all chat messages (no messages are private). 
Dlg TCPIP Host 7 Name                                       := Chat Message
Dlg TCPIP Host 7 Descr                                      := This edit box allows you to type in text to be sent to the other players and the host. Hit Enter or press the “Send” button to send the message. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 8 Name                                       := Send
Dlg TCPIP Host 8 Descr                                      := Sends the text in the Chat Message edit box to all of the other players. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 9 Name                                       := Wait For Players
Dlg TCPIP Host 9 Descr                                      := Begins the game and sends the game setup files to the players. Once each player connects they will be displayed in the Empire List. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 10 Name                                      := Begin Game
Dlg TCPIP Host 10 Descr                                     := Begins the game once all players have connected. When the game is begun, the first turn is generated and sent to all of the players. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 11 Name                                      := Process Turn
Dlg TCPIP Host 11 Descr                                     := After each player has taken their turn, an order file will be sent in to the host. Once all of the order files are received, the host presses the “Process Turn” button to process the next turn and have it sent to all of the players. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 12 Name                                      := Add Empire
Dlg TCPIP Host 12 Descr                                     := As players connect in to the host, the host can add additional empires to the game as human controlled or computer controlled. Any added human controlled empires must be played by the host. This action will display the Player Setup window to create the new empire. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 13 Name                                      := Remove Empire
Dlg TCPIP Host 13 Descr                                     := This button will remove the currently selected empire in the Empire List from the game. This may be needed if a player quits the game. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 14 Name                                      := Play Turn
Dlg TCPIP Host 14 Descr                                     := This button will allow display the Main Window so that the host can play a turn for the currently selected empire in the Empire List. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 15 Name                                      := Chat
Dlg TCPIP Host 15 Descr                                     := This action displays the Chat Messages List. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 16 Name                                      := Player List
Dlg TCPIP Host 16 Descr                                     := This action displays the Empire List. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 17 Name                                      := Select IP Address
Dlg TCPIP Host 17 Descr                                     := This will display a window to allow you to enter an IP address. This IP address will be used as the location for players to connect to. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 18 Name                                      := Select Port
Dlg TCPIP Host 18 Descr                                     := This will display a window to allow you to enter a port number. This port number will be the port used for communication by the players. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 19 Name                                      := Quit Game
Dlg TCPIP Host 19 Descr                                     := Quits the current game and closes this window. 
Dlg TCPIP Host 20 Name                                      := Select Modem
Dlg TCPIP Host 20 Descr                                     := This will display a window to allow you to select the modem for use in communications.

Dlg TCPIP Host 23 Descr                                     := The name of the player controlling this empire.

Dlg TCPIP Host 25 Descr                                     := The status of this player taking their turn.

Dlg Transfer Cargo 1 Name                                   := Transfer Cargo
Dlg Transfer Cargo 1 Descr                                  := The Transfer Cargo window allows you to transfer cargo between ships and planets. Only ships or planets in the same sector can transfer cargo.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 2 Name                                   := Cargo From List
Dlg Transfer Cargo 2 Descr                                  := Displays all of the vehicles and planets present in the current sector. Each ship or planet is followed by line items for each of the cargo items on it. Each vehicle or planet displays the current cargo space used out of the total amount of cargo space available. You can right click on any item in the list to get a report on it.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 3 Name                                   := Cargo To List
Dlg Transfer Cargo 3 Descr                                  := Displays all of the vehicles and planets in the sector that are not listed in the cargo From List. Both lists are interchangeable, and you can move items back and forth between them. This list displays items in the same manner as the Cargo From List. You can right click on any item in the list to get a report on it.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 4 Name                                   := Move Cargo Right
Dlg Transfer Cargo 4 Descr                                  := This action will move the currently selected cargo item from the Cargo From List to the current selected vehicle in the Cargo To List. The cargo will only be moved if there is sufficient cargo space available on the target vehicle.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 5 Name                                   := Move Ship Right
Dlg Transfer Cargo 5 Descr                                  := This action will move the currently selected vehicle in the Cargo From List to the Cargo To List.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 6 Name                                   := Amount
Dlg Transfer Cargo 6 Descr                                  := This selection indicates the amount of cargo items to move when you press the Move Cargo buttons. You can use the arrow buttons to increase and decrease the amount, or just click on the text and type in a number.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 7 Name                                   := Move Cargo Left
Dlg Transfer Cargo 7 Descr                                  := Same as the Move Cargo Right button except it moves cargo from the right list to the left list.
Dlg Transfer Cargo 8 Name                                   := Move Ship Left
Dlg Transfer Cargo 8 Descr                                  := Same as the Move Ship Right button except it moves vehicles from the right list to the left list

Dlg Transfer Cargo 9 Descr                                  := Closes the window.

Dlg Transfer Cargo 10 Descr                                 := Toggles whether the lists will display units individually or in summarized fashion.
